# WHAT'S NEW | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#jul-2025-bixgrow-3.1-charge-affiliate-membership-fees)

Jul 2025: BixGrow 3.1 – Charge affiliate membership fees


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’ve introduced Membership Plans – a new way to require affiliates to pay a joining fee. You can create multiple membership plans with different prices and link them to specific programs. Payments are collected via PayPal, and only verified transactions allow affiliates to join the selected program.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FMeIlJFjijunDR8GPRZvC%252FScreenshot_41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0aa77160-f326-4660-9ff2-bcedfbe1ac7e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5cd6f15c&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#jun-2025-bixgrow-3.1-new-import-options-indexing-control-and-automated-affiliate-gifts)

**Jun 2025: BixGrow 3.1 – New import options, indexing control, and automated affiliate gifts**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#enhanced-import-options)

✅ **Enhanced Import Options**

We’ve expanded our Import feature to support not just affiliates, but now also orders and coupons! This update is perfect for merchants who are switching from another affiliate platform to BixGrow, easily migrate your existing data and get up and running in no time.

⚠️To access them, please contact our support team, and we’ll help unlock the import tools based on your needs.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FZajq52iQ2MjYc4XzR9P5%252FScreenshot_35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff1851c2-e05d-4f40-abb2-666e825a8815&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d33bb4d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FFHEmUXDKj3xncveY3g9i%252FScreenshot_36.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5167ceb9-4cea-4aed-950a-f9da870c3e98&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c893cebf&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FItS8jXwauhMWbFf8ba0j%252FScreenshot_37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42934bcc-c16e-460a-9d83-88d78de3df98&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ae255c49&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#prevent-indexing)

✅ **Prevent indexing**

You now have the option to hide your affiliate portal from search engines. This helps protect your portal from being discovered by people you don’t intend to share it with.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FwiThrBEPHvgKxr7eglxV%252FScreenshot_38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde03fcab-f944-4e67-af6e-1161b9f9fd43&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=474cbc8d&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#gifts-feature)

🎁 **Gifts feature**

The new Gift options let you reward your affiliates with a free product or a discount code to use on their own orders. It can also be auto-generated for convenience.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FnVtMZ4fTAFw4ssLTV0O9%252FScreenshot_39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a1a4c61-6196-4015-9c63-9745879a2e96&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=decfe435&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FfU7EcTkThHE6GCzBa3z5%252FScreenshot_40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6fa884d-1d3e-498d-ba96-2fc7aa441f0c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=608de736&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#jan-2025-bixgrow-3.1-new-coupons-tab)

Jan 2025: BixGrow 3.1 - New Coupons tab


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’re excited to announce a new update to the Coupons tab in our app! Now, managing your coupons is easier than ever.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#comprehensive-coupon-list)

✅ **Comprehensive coupon list**

Access a detailed list of all your coupons with full information for seamless management.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FtIGs85BRxbpUZzdJ1MnM%252FScreenshot_1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad9fc286-5ea1-4bc9-bf7a-14951c56dda8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=37ae311e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#template-management)

✅ **Template management**

For coupons generated via a program or in bulk, a coupon template is now created to manage all associated codes. Easily view the total number of codes, edit the coupon format, and update their values.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FahWH8gALLURK0zsF4WKq%252FScreenshot_2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D683c7661-287a-4c60-9f08-2949564ae247&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12f7ebb5&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#id-30-oct-2024-bixgrow-3.1-new-way-to-work-with-coupons)

30 Oct 2024: BixGrow 3.1 - New way to work with Coupons


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#id-1.-program-page-reorganization)

1\. Program page reorganization

We’ve made it easier to navigate the Program page by organizing it into three clear sections: Commission Rules, Customer Discount, and Settings. This new layout simplifies the setup process, allowing you to manage your programs with ease.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F5GEHgpoDJ52AUZHPUHLB%252Fimage%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb02719e-3218-48f9-964b-19ddd83f32e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=773c2a50&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#id-2.-dynamic-coupon-feature)

2\. Dynamic coupon feature

Say goodbye to coupon leakage! The new Dynamic Coupon feature generates a unique, one-time-use coupon for each customer purchase made through an affiliate link.

**Available Coupon Types:**

\[Existing\] Static Coupon: A fixed code that affiliates can share with their audience.

\[New\] Dynamic Coupon: Automatically generated per click on an affiliate link, ensuring only eligible customers receive a discount and preventing unauthorized sharing.

To set up customer discounts, go to **Program > Edit Program > Customer Discount**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FlUP8fAlMHR5LE2hbte5X%252FScreenshot_247.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb6bf9a9-9e97-4076-9261-3e4615790e84&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c63fdff5&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#id-3.-upgraded-on-site-content-with-discount-popup)

3\. Upgraded on-site content with discount popup

A new discount popup feature highlights affiliate names and their discount offers, making these deals more noticeable to customers. This tool helps affiliates attract attention to promotions, encouraging more conversions

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FAP8o8Cb3FgrP1xJoeGvR%252FScreenshot_248.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24f7f52b-27df-4642-8457-5a51a085cfba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e04e2539&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#id-20-may-2024-bixgrow-3.0-the-newer-the-better)

20 May 2024: BixGrow 3.0 - the newer the better!


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/#id-1.-sleek-new-look)

1\. **Sleek new look**

We're revamping our UI to align with the Shopify Design system. Say hello to a fresh UI that will not only help you open the app faster and get an overview of your setups at first glance but is also super intuitive to use!

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FaohwPojfcVaqRQ0BNjvo%252FUntitled.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da852b60e-2ffc-4061-bf59-14ae9429ccc4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5c5416ef&sv=2)

Just take a look at our brand-new seamless design, isn't it a total match?

# What is BixGrow? | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

BixGrow is a Shopify app that simplifies the process of connecting merchants and affiliates, allowing merchants to easily manage their affiliate marketing activities. BixGrow's user-friendly interface allows merchants to easily set up and monitor affiliate programs. Meanwhile, affiliates gain access to a carefully curated marketplace of opportunities, enabling them to effectively monetize their influence.

One of the key advantages of an affiliate program is that it offers a low-cost, low-risk marketing solution—merchants only pay a portion of the sales revenue as commission once a sale has been made, ensuring that costs are tied directly to performance. To track referral orders, BixGrow provides affiliates with trackable links. Whenever someone makes a purchase through one of these links, the affiliate earns a commission, ensuring transparent and accurate tracking of performance and rewards.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/what-is-bixgrow#what-are-the-differences-between-the-affiliate-and-referral-programs)

What are the differences between the Affiliate and Referral programs?

BixGrow offers two distinct programs: the **Affiliate Program** and the **Referral Program**. While both programs involve rewarding others for promoting your business, they serve different purposes and target different audiences.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F9tNxwTWYcPQTQn52QFCe%252Fdoc-5.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e97ad78-5c25-4512-90ae-9dd5f8827b3a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e8d69352&sv=2)

The Affiliate Program is best suited for businesses aiming to collaborate with professional marketers to reach a wider audience. Meanwhile, the Referral Program is ideal for leveraging your current customer base to grow your store organically through word-of-mouth.

[PreviousWHAT'S NEW](https://docs.bixgrow.com/)
[NextHow to install BixGrow](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/how-to-install-bixgrow)

# What is an affiliate program? | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FYLgtRmlxy4fcrHMyt3Ek%252Fwhat-is-affiliate-marketing-bixgrow.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9947334-30f0-4f86-b98e-b656114237d1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=754f72ab&sv=2)

With an affiliate program, more potential customers can engage with your products and more easily. You must only pay once there are referral orders, thus lowering the risk.

_In this example, you recruited influencer A as an affiliate. A promotes your products on his YouTube channel and customers use the affiliate coupons he gives to place orders. As A successfully made referral orders, you pay him commissions._

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/what-is-an-affiliate-program#roles-in-an-affiliate-program)

Roles in an affiliate program


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are three parties: **Merchant**, **Affiliate**, and **Customer**. The customer pays for the products. Both merchant and affiliate receive a portion of that money by following a win-win situation where the merchant can increase revenue and the affiliate receives a commission.

*   **Merchant:** A merchant in an affiliate program's role is to set up and manage the program. This includes recruiting affiliates, defining commission structures, providing marketing materials, and tracking affiliate sales. Merchants are responsible for paying affiliates and optimizing the program to increase sales.
    
*   **Affiliate:** Affiliates promote the merchant’s products using unique links or coupons to drive traffic and sales. They create content to engage their audience, sharing these promotions on blogs, social media, or websites. Affiliates earn commissions based on the sales or leads they generate.
    
*   **Customer:** The buyer who purchases a product through an affiliate asset. They may receive special offers or discounts, driving sales for the merchant and earning commissions for the affiliate.
    

[PreviousCommon Terms](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/common-terms)
[NextCreate a program](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/create-a-program)

# How to install BixGrow | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

**Step 1: Install BixGrow from Shopify**

First, log in to your Shopify store and click "Add apps", then search for "BixGrow" to start the installation. Follow the prompts to complete the process, and BixGrow will be added to your Shopify dashboard.

⭐Start earning referrals from today! ⭐ [**Install now**](https://apps.shopify.com/bixgrow-affiliate-marketing?utm_source=bixgrow&utm_medium=organic)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fthiirg2AixnHnZZfVeuc%252FScreenshot_210.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dce895bd8-2e81-4269-b4fe-438ddec802bc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b59cf4&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FhNTh1fn3NQuo24UczN5Z%252FScreenshot_211.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D954e5fbd-4a2d-4d69-a46e-0da9f370ad97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9801accc&sv=2)

**Step 2: Choose the Right Program for Your Store**

After installation, you’ll need to decide which program—Affiliate or Referral—fits your store’s needs.

💡Let's explore what sets them apart. 💡[**Click here**](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/what-is-bixgrow#what-are-the-differences-between-the-affiliate-and-referral-programs)

*   **Affiliate Program**: Upon installation, BixGrow will guide you through an onboarding process. This includes creating affiliate programs, setting up commission rates, and customizing your affiliate portal. This program is recommended if you want to work with influencers or affiliates to drive significant traffic to your store.
    

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FwSXByk2dBZ2HKJKYfYQk%252FScreenshot_212.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a462243-6fb4-429b-85a0-8ea5fca662c3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec80ee9b&sv=2)

*   **Referral Program**: To access the Referral Program, go to the "Extra Functions" tab within BixGrow. Here, you can set up a system where your existing customers are encouraged to refer new customers in exchange for rewards. This program is much simpler to set up compared to the Affiliate program. This program is ideal if you want to focus on building customer loyalty and expanding your store’s reach organically.
    

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FVMfs4KNCMjoA1X3ybxhL%252FScreenshot_214.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3625567-ff13-4316-9429-3d58e69434ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=47f7f79e&sv=2)

By choosing the right program, you can maximize the effectiveness of BixGrow in growing your business through strategic marketing efforts.

# Common Terms | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FxBRDms1F1HXs4FU5PGlx%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a6b95760&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/common-terms#id-1.-affiliate-portal)

**1\. Affiliate Portal**

A page that can later be embedded into your store to recruit affiliates for your program. It can either be a landing page to give a quick explanation of how your program works, a sign-up page, or a log-in page for your affiliates.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/common-terms#id-2.-affiliate-program)

**2\. Affiliate Program**

A group that helps you categorize and manage affiliates with ease. You can set a default commission rate for each program. There are also many advanced program settings for special commission rules!

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/common-terms#id-3.-referral-order)

**3\. Referral Order**

A successful order brought by an affiliate.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/common-terms#id-4.-affiliate-link)

**4\. Affiliate Link**

Links that are respectively auto-generated when affiliates join the program and will then be used to promote.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/common-terms#id-5.-coupon)

**5\. Coupon**

Another means for your affiliates to promote besides links.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/common-terms#id-6.-network-commission)

**6\. Network** **Commission**

The commission affiliates receive when the downlines they recruited to the Multi-level Marketing network bring back orders.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/common-terms#id-7.-cookie)

**7\. Cookie**

The customers' information, such as purchasing habits and website preferences left when they visit your store.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/common-terms#id-8.-cookie-duration)

**8\. Cookie Duration**

**Cookie Duration** is the maximum number of days (typically 30-90 days) between the last click and the order, at which the affiliate will get a commission for the referral order. As long as that customer uses the same device and browser, and no other affiliate link or coupon is used when the order is placed, the cookie won't be overwritten and will give the respective affiliate a commission!

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FUKuwAlGTv3WfIvl8fmjf%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7ac7d4c&sv=2)

For example, you set the cookie duration to 30 days. Thus, within 30 days, the customer places an order even if not via an affiliate link, the respective affiliate will receive a commission. **NO** **conversions** will be recorded if the customer purchases not via an affiliate link from day 31 onwards.

[](https://docs.uppromote.com/basic-knowledge/affiliate-marketing-definition)

[PreviousHow to install BixGrow](https://docs.bixgrow.com/bixgrow-intro/how-to-install-bixgrow)
[NextWhat is an affiliate program?](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/what-is-an-affiliate-program)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Lifetime commission | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

If a customer is referred by an affiliate for the first time (the customer places the first order via an affiliate link/coupon), a link between them will be stored. Next time, when the same customer places another order (even without using the same affiliate link/coupon or device/browser), **BixGrow** can still identify the affiliate who originally referred this customer and give him a commission. The affiliate will continue to receive commissions for this customer's orders until his **Lifetime duration** ends.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/lifetime-commission#id-1.-how-to-enable-lifetime-commission)

1\. How to enable Lifetime commission


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set up a **Lifetime commission** for your program, you must first go to **Program** > **Edit** \> **Lifetime commission**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FEV4kbNp8ZUN22LdgoNOa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbdc456ac-cbdc-4943-ae8c-5935cd75fa66&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28f1cbbb&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F4gBYLoMIIEk7dkFWOJK4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba0df78e-309c-4f3d-a9f9-1fe8c818d076&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c1960b25&sv=2)

Once **Lifetime commission** is enabled, all existing links between affiliates and customers in the **Conversions** \> **Customers** tab will become lifetime links. In this example, affiliate Lilly Howe brought customer James to your store. Since you set up **Lifetime commission**, all subsequent orders from James regardless of the affiliate links he uses will be credited to Lilly.

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/lifetime-commission#id-2.-lifetime-duration)

2\. Lifetime duration


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Next, you can also decide on **Lifetime duration** - if it's valid forever, or for a limited time only.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FkQ2BI3VKcRbJlA9exFWZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e1d093e-e555-4b77-a27f-aaae6656c83f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a30ab6bd&sv=2)

In this example, **Lifetime commission** is limited to 60 days, which means the links between affiliates and their customers will expire after 60 days. These customers will have to use affiliate links/coupons in order for affiliates to be credited for commissions again.

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/lifetime-commission#id-3.-lifetime-commission-amount)

**3\. Lifetime commission amount**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Lifetime commission** amount is the commission amount given to affiliates for subsequent orders. By default, it is the **default commission**. You can apply another commission amount by going to [**Advanced commission setup**](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/advanced-commission-rules)
.

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/lifetime-commission#id-4.-manually-link-unlink-an-affiliate-with-a-customer)

**4\. Manually link/unlink an affiliate with a customer**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can link an affiliate with a customer to create a **Lifetime commission** link between them even before the customer places the first order. To do so, you must first go to the **Conversions** tab > **Customers** and then click this **Link customer** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FdmJKcb7Meh7Ns0lL48a7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da9ff2a8c-09ce-4dbc-b1ba-36d89af36aed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0446147&sv=2)

Now select the affiliate and search for/add the customer you want to link. Finally, click **Save**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F1SSKF6YYsvmayR8wc03M%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9eb4d647-4f60-437b-85a9-41c28599c889&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1f23e08&sv=2)

To manually unlink the affiliate and the customer, simply click this **Delete** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FrG6ZNy9rtXwKXJzboZ5R%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df398de4a-d5d7-446f-8e27-67f8c98bc505&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=739ffb90&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/lifetime-commission#faq)

FAQ


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q**: How is **Lifetime commission** different from **Cookie**?

**A**: **Lifetime commission** has an override ability while **Cookie** doesn't.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/lifetime-commission#example)

Example

During a **Lifetime commission duration**, no affiliate link/coupon usage can replace it at all. If customer A is linked to affiliate B with an in-effect **Lifetime commission**, no matter if A places an order using affiliate C's link, or affiliate D's coupon - all orders will still be credited to B. This only stops once the **Lifetime commission** expires. While during a **Cookie duration**, any affiliate link/coupon usage can replace it even though the **Cookie** is still active. If customer A uses affiliate B's link first but then places an order using affiliate C's link, or affiliate D's coupon - these orders will be credited to C and D respectively.

[PreviousSpecial product commission](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/special-product-commission)
[NextOther advanced commission rules](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/advanced-commission-rules)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Create a program | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

You can create various programs for affiliates with different commission rules, which helps you categorize and manage affiliates with ease.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/create-a-program#id-1.-how-to-create)

1\. How to create


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/create-a-program#a.-create-from-scratch)

**a. Create from scratch**

To create a new program, you can go to **Program** and click the **Create program** button in the top right corner.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FDPh8AiQ4su4VkXKQUxyz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ae7cfa1-4f61-4971-bf2b-3bad93e5b2a1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ae69f0e&sv=2)

There must be at least **ONE** program.

Next, give your program a descriptive title (you can always change this later) and click **Create**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FQQlBn6sIJv412gSMyyN2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b4083c3-a2ff-438e-ad2e-7c9ff63e2ca7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13d51c86&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/create-a-program#b.-duplicate-a-program)

b. Duplicate a program

Duplicating a program copies its settings, but affiliates remain with the original program, preserving your existing affiliate relationships and performance metrics.

To duplicate a program, you can go to **Program**, choose the program you want to duplicate and then click the three dots in the upper right hand corner and click the **Duplicate this program** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FIDtpKdgMb2uYG75VB3Va%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4838c781-ac5f-4c65-9bd9-2ce3f5e2b9a2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7743997c&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/create-a-program#id-2.-set-up-a-default-commission)

2\. Set up a Default commission


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Default commission** is the commission given to all affiliates in the program when they successfully bring orders. You can choose between **Percent of sales**, **Fixed amount per order**, or **Fixed amount per item**.

To set up the default commission rate for your program, go to **Program** > **Edit**, there in the **Edit** page, you will find the **Commission rules** section.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FyTAzi1WQ8KIiJDfMtClD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5941ff7d-87c5-492f-8623-70eff62eeae4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2e47d771&sv=2)

*   **Percent of sale** is a certain percentage of the order's total sales.
    

_For example, if you set the commission rate to 10% of sale, your affiliates will receive 10% of the order's total sales each time they bring back orders._

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/create-a-program#faq)

FAQ


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/create-a-program#what-commission-rate-should-i-offer-affiliates)

What commission rate should I offer affiliates?

Affiliate commission rates can vary greatly depending on the niche, the products and services being promoted, or the affiliate program in use. Here are some recommended ranges of commission rates for different niches:

Niche

Recommended commission rate

Fashion

5-15%

Beauty

15-20%

Jewelry

15-30%

Health & Wellness

10-30%

Fitness

10-20%

Home & Garden

10-20%

Baby

5-15%

Food & Beverages

5-20%

Pets

10-20%

Sexual Wellness

10-15%

However, please keep in mind that this is just our recommendation. It's best to calculate and decide your affiliate commission rate based on your own store's profit margins. To make sure that commissions are calculated on the exact base you want, please set up Commissionable Sales!

*   **Fixed amount per order** is a fixed amount for every order.
    

_For example, if you set the commission rate to $3 per order, your affiliates will receive $3 each time they bring back orders regardless of the orders' value._

*   **Fixed amount per item** is a fixed amount for every item of the order.
    

_For example, if you set the commission rate to $3 per item, your affiliates will receive $6 each time they bring back orders of 2 items._

*   **Tiers** are different commission rates for different affiliates based on their all-time personal sales performance. Tiers can be reset so that all affiliates will start at the same tier after a certain cycle.
    

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F7Z3yrZx6tE2ByihAq9zL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6ecb1961-8ea8-4c59-8e0d-a9dd1150002a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57778ee9&sv=2)

[NextSelect products to be applicable for commissions](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/applicable-products-for-commissions)

# Special product commission | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

To set up a **Special product commission**, you must go to **Program** > **Edit** and click the **Add product** button under **Special product commission** section.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F6Wu02F0WNNN8tqRnxho6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D491a6a81-b315-4749-afe2-8b7446b3c8b2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ecd89aa5&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/special-product-commission#example)

**Example**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F9BtBvGuV4zeekMbSCWXI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38d289bc-27ae-467b-ba12-dec29b2049ba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5d7a6ba&sv=2)

Here are some examples of combinations of **Special product commission** and **Default commission** within the same order:

*   If your default commission type is **Percent of sale**:
    

_Product A ($30) gives a 20% commission and the default commission is 10%, so when a customer places an order of product A and product B ($100), the commission to be given will be: $30x20% + $100x10% = $16._

*   If your default commission type is **Fixed amount per order**:
    

_Product A ($30) gives a 20% commission and the default commission is $15 per order, so when a customer places an order of product A and product B, the commission to be given will be: $30x20% + $15 = $21._

You can also **sync**, **edit** or **delete** the **Special product commission** by clicking these three **Actions** buttons.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FR4mZA91Oq7QmOnjDJQz8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Defe9818b-c283-4480-9d5c-d1eefb17700b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d894e8cd&sv=2)

In case you select **Specific collections**, please click the **Sync** button to re-sync the collection when new products are added to it on Shopify.

# Select products to be applicable for commissions | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

To set up **Product selection**, you must first go to **Program** > **Edit** > **Product selection**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FrpIeT4WN8cvfqNqpEzME%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87745980-9ec2-4a26-8e67-7ac3976565d5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7422350f&sv=2)

*   **All products/collections**: All products or collections in your Shopify store are eligible for commission.
    
*   **Specific products/collections**: Only specific products or collections will be eligible for commission. If you want to give commission only on some specific products or collections, please select this and purchases of products not on the list won't be tracked.
    

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F0aqGr6Cd7RglmuPcvfpn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e5304e0-36b5-4f70-bed8-f413d5a4e7d2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9c5e5559&sv=2)

In this example, affiliates in this program can only earn commissions on two products: _Yellow Wool Jumper_ and _Floral White Top_.

*   **All products/collections except**: All products or collections except those listed here are eligible for commission. If you want to exclude commission only for some specific products or collections, please select this and purchases of products on the list won't be tracked.
    

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FNan8UBmDOS4VfPY9E0Q5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da285f7fa-8e37-4461-a4c1-fc8674d8419d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ab816a74&sv=2)

In this example, affiliates in this program can earn commissions on all products except the two listed: _Yellow Wool Jumper_ and _Floral White Top_.

In case you select **Specific collections**, please click the **Sync** button to re-sync the collection when new products are added to it on Shopify.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FISlt5LkXMDeuFMl3gW7V%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3bf3c497-adae-493d-9931-eda039a2fab3&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=83362b50&sv=2)

# Commissionable sales | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

**Commissionable sale** is the sale value that BixGrow uses to calculate your affiliates' commission. It may be the same sale value as shown on Shopify, or the actual sale **including discounts/shipping fees/taxes** depending on your selection.

Please note that the discount value is a **negative number** by default (for example a $20 discount will become -20 in the **Commissionable sales** **calculation**).

To set up **Commissionable sales**, kindly navigate to **Settings** > **General**.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commissionable-sales#id-1.-includes-discounts)

**1\. Includes Discounts**

If the **Discounts** checkbox is selected, the **commissionable sale** will be calculated by **subtracting** the discount value from the actual order's sale. This means that your affiliates' commission amount will **decrease** if the commission rule is **Percent of sale**. For other commission rules, the commission amount is not affected.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Flxuw4x1dDzLbluw8VFyt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a912fd2-2de4-410a-a43a-7dba50ffd0c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=66c43d6e&sv=2)

In this example, if a customer places an order of $100 ($20 discount), the **commissionable sale** will be $100-20 = $80. The affiliate's program commission is 10% of sale, therefore it will be 10% of $80 = **$8**.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commissionable-sales#id-2.-includes-shipping-fees)

**2\. Includes shipping fees**

If the **Shipping** checkbox is selected, the **commissionable sale** will be calculated by **adding** the shipping fee from the actual order's sale. This means that your affiliates' commission amount will **increase** if the commission rule is **Percent of sale**. For other commission rules, the commission amount is not affected.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FeVFMDZ5giZxKLWCCawA9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dabf92633-332a-4f8d-9c0a-5b6280ea8b44&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=27316141&sv=2)

In this example, if a customer places an order of $100 ($10 shipping), the **commissionable sale** will be $100+10 = $110. The affiliate's program commission is 10% of sale, therefore it will be 10% of $110 = **$11**.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commissionable-sales#id-3.-includes-taxes)

**3\. Includes taxes**

If the **Tax** checkbox is selected, the **commissionable sale** will be calculated by **adding** the tax from the actual order's sale. This means that your affiliates' commission amount will i**ncrease** if the commission rule is **Percent of sale**. For other commission rules, the commission amount is not affected.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F6dEvD92asYQMEwO6JHT3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbec15422-da95-488c-9d10-89da7bf3733d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f5f1d79d&sv=2)

In this example, if a customer places an order of $100 ($5 tax), the **commissionable sales** will be $100+5 = $105. The affiliate's program commission is 10% of sale, therefore it will be 10% of $105 = **$10,5**.

[PreviousCommission priority](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commission-priority)
[NextInvite/Add/Import affiliates](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/add-invite-import-affiliates)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Commission priority | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commission-priority#id-1.-between-tracking-methods)

1\. Between tracking methods


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As you've known, 2 tracking methods can be used to calculate your affiliates' commission: **by link** or **coupon**. However, under any circumstances, **only ONE** will take effect. Therefore you **won't** give two commission types within an order even if you enable both tracking types and customers use both affiliate links and coupons to place orders. In case both are used, the order will be tracked **by coupon** and will give the affiliate a coupon commission only.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commission-priority#tracking-by-coupon-greater-than-tracking-by-link)

**Tracking by coupon > Tracking by link**.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commission-priority#id-2.-between-commission-types)

2\. Between commission types


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In case many commission types are applied to the same referral at the same time, **only ONE** will take effect and the order will be tracked by the one that comes first as below:

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commission-priority#lifetime-commission-greater-than-special-commissions-greater-than-default-commission)

**Lifetime commission > Special commissions > Default commission**.

[PreviousRoyalty](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/royalty)
[NextCommissionable sales](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commissionable-sales)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Other advanced commission rules | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

To set up **Advanced commission rules** for your program, you must first go to **Program** > **Edit** > **Show advanced commission setups**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Ft7aMENay9CP0W0B4GcdQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8514706a-f379-4dc8-97bc-fdd705c1e8d8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=409622a9&sv=2)

Type

Condition

Meaning

Example

**Coupon**

**Affiliate coupon**

Apply to orders using coupons assigned to affiliates.

If the **Coupon** is an **Affiliate coupon**, the commission amount of orders with coupons assigned to affiliates applied will be W%

**Any coupon**

Apply to all orders using coupons created by **BixGrow** or Shopify

If the **Coupon** is an **Any coupon**, the commission amount of orders with any coupons applied will be X%

**Equal to**

Only apply to orders using the coupon whose name equal to the inserted value

If the **Coupon** is **Equal to** A, the commission amount of orders with the coupon named A applied will be Y% (coupon code A = Y% commission)

**Contains**

Apply to orders using coupons that contain the inserted value

If the **Coupon contains** A, the commission amount of orders with the coupons whose name contains A applied will be Z% (coupon code A/AAA/ABC,... = Z% commission)

**Disable tracking**

Apply to all orders that meet this condition and not give commissions for them

If the **Coupon** is **Disable tracking**, all orders with this **Coupon** condition met will not be tracked nor given any commissions

**Customer**

**New**

Apply to orders placed by customers that have never purchased before

If the **Customer** is **New**, the commission amount of orders placed by new customers will be X%

**Old**

Apply to orders placed by customers that have purchased before

If the **Customer** is **Old**, the commission amount of orders placed by old customers will be Y%

**Disable tracking**

Apply to all orders that meet this condition and not give commissions for them

If the **Customer** is **Old** and **Disable tracking**, all orders placed by old customers will not be tracked nor given any commissions

**Lifetime tracking**

Apply to subsequent orders of linked customers after **Lifetime commission** is enabled in **Settings**

If **Lifetime commission amount for subsequent orders** is set up as X%, the commission that affiliates receive for their subsequent orders will be X%

If an order meets more than one condition set up in **Advanced commission rule**, only the rule with higher priority will be applied. You can change their priority by rearranging the rules.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FtbhCGdqTfpF495EsfQs1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17d3aa7a-fcd2-49e4-b95b-9a0b303f20ba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a21b444a&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/advanced-commission-rules#faqs)

FAQs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q1:** I'm having a holiday sale in my store and don't want to pay commissions on orders that have HOLIDAY discounts applied. How do I set it up so that the app automatically cancels commissions in this case?

**A1:**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FVzenBCinWCqam3JeyUzx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f6c316b-ce99-4a85-b21b-fc1462296a21&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aaeec513&sv=2)

In this example, if the order has a coupon whose name contains "HOLIDAY" applied, it will not be tracked nor given any commissions.

**Q2:** I want to give affiliates a 10% commission for bringing new customers but only 5% if it's old customers that they bring. How do I set it up so that the app automatically gives different commission amounts for these customer groups?

**A2:**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fjs1TKwWYuBuADhWtW1D9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77ab191f-fd95-4f5b-bf5a-b5fac608e377&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fcc830d6&sv=2)

In this example, if the customer is old, the commission will be 5% \[Please keep in mind that a **default commission** (for new customers) must be set up as 10% first. You can also achieve the same result if setting up the **default commission** as 5% and the **advanced commission rule** as Customer - New - 10% here.\]

**Q3.** I want to use Lifetime tracking, but only if I can make Lifetime Commission gradually decrease after each order is created. How do I set it up so that the Lifetime Commission is 10% for the first order and 5% for subsequent orders?

**A3:** To be able to set up different commissions based on Lifetime tracking, **Lifetime commission** must first be [enabled](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/lifetime-commission#how-to-set-up)
.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FacAU5Q2SRDJ8DigwiWR3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc47d7309-c47d-422c-85a4-3ea7340777f8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=423122de&sv=2)

In this example, the commission that affiliates receive for their subsequent orders will be 5% (please keep in mind that a **default commission** must be set up as 10% first).

[PreviousLifetime commission](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/lifetime-commission)
[NextRoyalty](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/royalty)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Royalty | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

**Royalty** allows your affiliates to benefit from all subsequent orders with **linked products/collections** included, therefore making a great incentive for affiliates to promote your business. Also, with **Royalty**, there is no need for a link/coupon or cookie for BixGrow to track which affiliate is attributed to the commission!

The **Royalty** feature can be found in **Extra functions** > **Others** > **Royalty**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FTGh9PG2mEPAc5DPKhVLe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7dc954c0-18e6-41c5-93b9-1b951b10fe03&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=162cf5c3&sv=2)

To link a product/collection to an affiliate, you must first click this **Link product** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FKSe4rjAVudpHUzOa9AIY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df46875ce-2794-40b2-b7cd-0c53cfe3798e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cf7ac506&sv=2)

Now select the affiliate and search for the product/collection and variants you want to link. You can also set a custom commission for this.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fi88QgkUnT17490J5pFTC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee32fba0-a3cb-48eb-bd71-81bb519ff07d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3dc7e2ca&sv=2)

Each product/collection can only be linked to **ONE** affiliate.

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/royalty#faq)

FAQ


--------------------------------------------------------------------

**Q:** When I link a product to affiliate A in Royalty, will a regular affiliate B get paid if their referral order includes that product?

**A:** Yes, in that case, affiliate B who refers the order receives commission (default program commission), and affiliate A receives royalty commission.

[PreviousOther advanced commission rules](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/advanced-commission-rules)
[NextCommission priority](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commission-priority)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Invite/Add/Import affiliates | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/add-invite-import-affiliates#id-1.-invite-affiliates)

1\. Invite affiliates


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To invite affiliates to join your program, you must first navigate to the **BixGrow** tab and click the **Copy** Sign-up page button under the **Affiliate portal links** section.

Now, share the page link where potential affiliates can find and sign up for your program (e.g., on your storefront, via social media, etc.).

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F9SKB9mjaNfjn1OAydppy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9aa5cc0f-649c-4ae9-a72a-aafc7091438a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71b6cb6e&sv=2)

* * *

Typically, potential affiliates can find the **sign-up page** and complete the form to sign up for your program. However, you can **add** or **import** **affiliates** directly if you have a pre-existing list of affiliates.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/add-invite-import-affiliates#id-2.-add-an-affiliate-manually)

2\. Add an affiliate manually


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To manually add affiliates to your program, you must first click the **Add affiliate** button in the **Affiliates** tab.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FXLR004jmAF0RVY09ZrYk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D679b5f1a-1898-4a0d-b74f-013b806c1655&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ee78ad00&sv=2)

1.  Select the program you want to add the affiliate to
    
2.  Fill in basic information (name, email)
    
3.  Fill in a password of your choice, or select the auto-generated password
    
4.  (Optional) Select **Send an invitation email** (this is the **Added affiliates** template that includes the affiliate's log-in link and password and can be edited in **Email** \> **Email notifications** \> **Added affiliates** \> **Edit**)
    
5.  Click **Save**
    

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FJJ1vSMZcljc7fWytfTf3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0bb4c26f-fc7e-4048-ae62-ce211463805b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=daa6c056&sv=2)

We highly recommend you check the **Send invitation email** checkbox, as it will be easier for you to resend in case the email didn't reach its recipient, or if you don't remember the set password.

Now the affiliate has been added to your program.

* * *

To reduce manual tasks, you can **bulk-import** affiliates into your programs.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/add-invite-import-affiliates#id-3.-bulk-import-affiliates)

3\. Bulk import affiliates


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can bulk import up to 10,000 affiliates (maximally 250 per file and 2,000 per day) into your programs. This is extremely useful when you migrate from another app.

This feature is **enabled upon request for eligible users only**. We require a verified email domain, a legit affiliate account list, and a subscription to a paid plan.

To do so, you must first contact us to enable the **Import** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F4GG7MTPLwxSGFNYP8lgp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62c404c2-8fa0-4ed7-933c-1f81204eb820&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=892e43f0&sv=2)

1.  Upload your CSV file (_first\_name, last\_name_, and _email_ columns are required).
    
2.  Select the program you want to import affiliates into.
    
3.  Fill in a default password of your choice (if your CSV file already includes the password, please skip this step).
    
4.  Choose to **send an invitation email** including the affiliate's log-in link and password or not.
    
5.  Click **Import affiliate**
    

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FOW3poNtQwfubyh22qBwf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06ed108b-8c81-405f-aa37-c728f34103db&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=162dde1&sv=2)

**Download our sample CSV file** to set up your data field columns correctly!

Only affiliates' **personal information** included in this list can be imported: first\_name, last\_name, email, password, country, company, address, city, zipcode, state, phone, facebook, instagram, youtube, twitter, website.

**Affiliate coupons** and **referral orders** require separate import files and can't be imported here along with affiliate accounts.

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/add-invite-import-affiliates#faq)

FAQ


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Q: Why am I unable to invite more affiliates to join my program/Why are my affiliates appear to be **Blocked**?

A: The maximum number of affiliates you can have on our **Starter** (free) plan is 30. Once you have reached that limit, you will not be able to have any more affiliates.

[PreviousCommissionable sales](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-programs/commissionable-sales)
[NextUse the Sign-up page](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/use-the-sign-up-page)

# Export affiliates | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/manage-affiliates/export-affiliates#id-1.-export-all-affiliates)

1\. Export all affiliates


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To export all affiliates, you must first click the **Export** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FCm5SH7WmrAGOqo4Bg2oy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45efbba5-3331-4d98-ab6b-15889f08e458&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3323fbbf&sv=2)

Then select **All affiliates** and click **Export**. You will have an Excel file that contains all of your affiliates' information.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FJjQsB9WjC68IklEclIn1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0265eb8-7324-4c17-9bb7-bc69431d0ade&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50b5dcb5&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/manage-affiliates/export-affiliates#id-2.-export-specific-affiliates)

2\. Export specific affiliates


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To export specific affiliates based on **name**, **status**, or **program**, you must first apply the filters you want.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FJxG0qWZs2LfgBclafB3s%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4c86b69-138b-417d-bdb4-28765cd38e2d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b178688f&sv=2)

Next, click this **Export** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FwrAhFnJBifzw6ccrPZLv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05461fe3-2495-457e-93c8-8e26a557c84a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5cbfe86&sv=2)

Then select **Filtered affiliates** and click **Export**. You will have a CSV file that contains all of your filtered affiliates' information.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FJlCt1nfkYPSwblTxDddl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e31ce60-0437-421f-bb80-b7c76d85f68b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c5ff3019&sv=2)

# How to disable or limit user to sign up | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/use-the-sign-up-page/how-to-disable-or-limit-user-to-sign-up#id-1.-lock-sign-up-page)

1\. Lock Sign-up page


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This feature disables your program's **sign-up page** and requires you to manually add affiliates to the program.

To enable this feature for your program, you must first go to **Programs** > **Edit** \> **Settings** > **Lock Sign-up page**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FRuWVJYRPjMZaGSIJkzGG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73499d52-e91e-4852-9bca-a75523e71431&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=38d0b24b&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/use-the-sign-up-page/how-to-disable-or-limit-user-to-sign-up#id-2.-limit-sign-up-by-location)

2\. Limit sign-up by location


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This feature restricts sign-ups to specific countries or regions, allowing you to make your program only available to affiliates in those areas.

To enable this feature for your program, you must first go to **Programs** > **Edit** \> **Settings** > **Limit affiliate sign-up** **by location**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FO59JKQlQalyrstqfiDYm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deaa2ba69-0cdd-409e-9e87-b58515e493a4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4ac5c5d3&sv=2)

This is highly recommended if your store doesn't offer worldwide shipping!

[PreviousMultiple sign-up pages](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/use-the-sign-up-page/multiple-sign-up-pages)
[NextManage Affiliates](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/manage-affiliates)

# Track affiliate link clicks | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

The **Click tracking** feature allows you to view a list of **clicks** on all **affiliate links.** There are the click's date, insights (customer's used device, browser and OS), the affiliate whose link was clicked, referrer URL (if the link was clicked on another site and not directly accessed - for example, Facebook), and destination URL which is the exact link that was clicked.

To view the **Clicks** list, navigate to the **Conversions** tab > **Clicks**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FJRJEsnfA6lUtMSsZ8PQg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac22fc74-fb55-4112-8920-8324b0c6531e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d5fd87fb&sv=2)

You can also filter the results by date, affiliate, country.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F0xkHfPAvIegUAb6loRn1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da422f379-3fb8-42f3-9fde-1076ab38802c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6a0c22a7&sv=2)

[PreviousAuto-shortened link](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/auto-shortened-link)
[NextAdd UTM to affiliate links](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/add-utm-to-affiliate-links)

# Manage affiliate links | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Managing affiliate links effectively is crucial for both merchants and affiliates to ensure smooth operation and maximize the success of the affiliate program. In BixGrow, merchants and affiliates have various links and options for customizing, shortening, and managing affiliate links.

*   [Default affiliate link](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/default-affiliate-link)
    : When an affiliate signs up for your program through BixGrow, a default affiliate link is automatically generated. This link is unique to each affiliate and is usually based on the main URL of your store, with a tracking parameter appended to it.
    
*   [Product link](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/product-link)
    : Affiliate link to a specific product instead of your store's homepage.
    
*   [Custom link](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/custom-link)
    : Custom links offer both merchants and affiliates the flexibility to tailor links to specific campaigns.
    
*   [Auto-shortened link:](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/auto-shortened-link)
     BixGrow offers an auto-shorten feature for affiliate links, which is especially useful for merchants who want to simplify links automatically. When this feature is enabled, the default affiliate link is shortened automatically as soon as an affiliate signs up for your program.
    

[PreviousHow do affiliate links work?](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/how-do-affiliate-links-work)
[NextDefault affiliate link](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/default-affiliate-link)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Bonus for outstanding performances | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/motivate-affiliates/performance-bonus#id-1.-what-is-performance-bonus)

1\. What is Performance bonus?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Not many things could be accomplished without proper rewards - so does affiliate marketing. Getting your rewards right is essential because while finding new quality affiliates from scratch takes time and effort, keeping them motivated and engaged is often way easier and more cost-effective. **Performance bonus** has a huge impact on making sure affiliates will stay loyal and work harder on lending their trustworthy voices to promote your business. What merchant wouldn’t want to show gratitude to their affiliates for constantly bringing all those sales anyway?

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FbqjqJAIbeZVfwqRdj5z1%252Faf-motivate-af-bonus.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De693d165-f3d5-46a5-a92e-cdb5863512db&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6727f8c5&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/motivate-affiliates/performance-bonus#id-2.-how-to-set-up)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# How do affiliate links work? | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Affiliate links are a fundamental tool in affiliate marketing, provided to affiliates so they can share them with their audience. These links allow affiliates to earn commissions by driving traffic and sales to a merchant’s website.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/how-do-affiliate-links-work#how-affiliate-links-are-generated)

How affiliate links are generated


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When an affiliate signs up for your affiliate program through BixGrow, a unique default affiliate link is generated for them.

Affiliates can find their link by logging into their **Affiliate Dashboard**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FOHLqnYonjGldIWU6W65z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D617507e6-c31a-4286-ab2f-3247d219da02&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b01316c&sv=2)

Merchants can also view affiliate link in the app by clicking on the affiliate’s name in the **Affiliates** tab.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F2KUnsVDLkqxViFu9gwPh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D453266c3-e3d2-48f9-8a0b-72469a7bbaf3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fa54142b&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/how-do-affiliate-links-work#structure-of-an-affiliate-link)

Structure of an affiliate link

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FhkVM69W2788HkQh6IKzb%252Faf-tracking-method-link.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28aa1129-f376-471b-b543-d796421255ba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7844aee8&sv=2)

An affiliate link typically consists of two main components:

**Base URL**: This is the store’s URL, which can be the homepage or a specific product page that you want to promote.

E.g. [_https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com_](https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/)

**Uniquie tracking ID**: This is the unique identifier or tracking code that differentiates one affiliate’s link from another. It is usually appended to the base URL as a query parameter. BixGrow tracking parameters usually include _bg\_ref._

E.g. _?bg\_ref=VQ9q75ODfg_

This structure ensures that when a customer clicks on the affiliate link and makes a purchase, the sale is attributed to the correct affiliate, allowing them to earn a commission.

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/how-do-affiliate-links-work#how-does-tracking-and-commission-attribution-work)

How does tracking and commission attribution work?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a customer clicks on an affiliate link, a cookie is placed on their device. A cookie is a small piece of data that stores information about the customer's visit to your store. This cookie includes details like the affiliate's tracking parameter and the time of the click.

The cookie remains on the customer's device for a specified period, known as the cookie duration. If the customer returns to your store and makes a purchase within this period, the affiliate is credited with the sale, and the corresponding commission is attributed to them.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FdCzXvLkkgvnUGbGcMbEH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8721a081-4af2-453a-9c13-5fd61f768230&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=32e4b52d&sv=2)

_For example:_

A customer clicks on an affiliate link on August 1st, and a cookie with a 30-day duration is placed on their device. The customer revisits your store on August 15th and makes a purchase. Because the purchase occurred within the 30-day cookie duration, the affiliate who shared the link will earn a commission for the sale.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/how-do-affiliate-links-work#customizing-cookie-duration)

Customizing Cookie Duration

As a merchant, you have control over the cookie duration, allowing you to determine how long the affiliate’s link remains valid for commission attribution. The standard duration might be 30 days, but depending on your business model, you can adjust this to be longer or shorter.

Longer cookie durations may be beneficial for affiliates, as they increase the likelihood of earning commissions from customers who take longer to decide on a purchase. On the other hand, shorter durations might be preferred if you want to ensure commissions are attributed to more recent marketing efforts.

To adjust cookie duration, you can go to the **Settings** tab > **Affiliate link**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F8CzefEd5A4gon2WWLgFl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2cf6addf-2870-46ed-8cd1-62388a991d99&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=930f4ab6&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/how-do-affiliate-links-work#faq)

FAQ


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/how-do-affiliate-links-work#q-who-gets-the-commission-if-a-customer-clicks-on-multiple-affiliate-links-during-the-cookie-duratio)

Q: Who gets the commission if a customer clicks on multiple affiliate links during the cookie duration?

A: In the event that a customer clicks on multiple affiliate links during the cookie duration, the commission for the order will be attributed to the latest affiliate whose link was clicked.

Here's how it works:

*   When a customer first clicks on affiliate A's link, a cookie is placed on their device to track that affiliate's referral. If the customer later clicks on affiliate B's link before making a purchase, the original cookie is overwritten with affiliate B's information.
    
*   The commission for any resulting purchase will be credited to the most recent affiliate whose link was clicked, as their link is considered the last point of referral.
    

This ensures that the affiliate who had the most recent influence on the customer's decision is rewarded for the sale.

[PreviousGifts](https://docs.bixgrow.com/gifts)
[NextManage affiliate links](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links)

Last updated 4 months ago

# Move affiliates to another program | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/manage-affiliates/move-affiliates-to-another-program#id-1.-move-an-affiliate-to-another-program)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FDsnf6bMvhd2Nf6OS6zSM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a6161b5-405f-4c2f-94e3-a58edafd1ce3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=469c80b&sv=2)

# Approve/Deny/Delete an affiliate | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

By default, when an affiliate registers for your program, the request's status will be **pending** and needs to be reviewed manually (unless you enabled **Auto-approve affiliate**). Their affiliate accounts will be **inactive** so they can still log in, but all affiliate information will be hidden until you approve.

To approve/deny/delete an affiliate, you must first navigate to the **Affiliates** tab.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/manage-affiliates/approve-deny-delete-an-affiliate#id-1.-approve)

**1\. Approve**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To approve an affiliate request, you must click this **Approve** button under the **Action** column.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FsfOG1K92E4SF3nld36vN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13ab8381-dae5-4ffd-974c-429133310557&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a1b6918d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/manage-affiliates/approve-deny-delete-an-affiliate#id-2.-deny)

**2\. Deny**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To deny an affiliate request, you must click this **Deny** button under the **Action** column.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FTvtv38KgGdkwPGDYf2Gu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64e286f8-aaa5-4863-9a91-4f106f9e629b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c504a27&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/manage-affiliates/approve-deny-delete-an-affiliate#id-3.-delete)

**3\. Delete**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To delete an affiliate account, you must click this **Delete** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FT7oKkDiEaULjjvd549US%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0be9f6be-077a-4e94-a11f-005bc9881bcc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bd2c4a3e&sv=2)

Please keep in mind that when you delete an affiliate, any associated data (conversions, coupons,...) will be **removed** as well!
