# Auto-shortened link | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

BixGrow offers an auto-shorten feature for affiliate links, which is especially useful for merchants who want to simplify links automatically. When this feature is enabled, the default affiliate link is shortened automatically as soon as an affiliate signs up for your program.

To enable this feature, kindly navigate to **Settings** > **Affiliate Link** and then enable the **Auto-Shortened Link** option.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FtH70VkG1YQAyyBCHk3CU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6b1e7c5-8778-4c35-a45e-5b7d2c9d2522&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46a81e47&sv=2)

You must first set up the rules that our system can use to generate links following this format for your future affiliates. When an affiliate signs up for your program, his default affiliate link will be auto-shortened.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FeLXZrx2CRWEsEKsGDIj0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5fdc2252-438c-4e63-844a-7645f51cecca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dca03028&sv=2)

For example, with the template in the screenshot below, affiliate Evelyn Jones with the default affiliate link [https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/?bg\_ref=VQ9q75ODfg&utm\_source=aff](https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/?bg_ref=VQ9q75ODfg&utm_source=aff)
 will now have the auto-shortened link [https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/SPONGEEEVELYN](https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/?bg_ref=VQ9q75ODfg&utm_source=aff)
.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FWB1e5Lef7x1pqqB9mMSY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1176ade6-5231-454b-b87b-09b1edb1aa14&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28f77db2&sv=2)

This rule does **NOT** apply to existing affiliates.

[PreviousCustom link](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/custom-link)
[NextTrack affiliate link clicks](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/track-affiliate-link-clicks)

# Level up for higher commissions | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Affiliate tiers automatically move your affiliates to higher-commissioned programs when they meet the conditions you specified, thereby motivating them to earn more.

This feature is **version-based** to make sure you don't take it for **Commission tiers**. Please contact us if you need it enabled and are a **PRO** subscriber.

The **Affiliate tiers** feature can be found in **Extra functions** > **Motivate affiliates**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fe6xGWosyKbjBixZF23ee%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ebb46a1-86b7-45f1-af55-d9ad050d753b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8602d1b&sv=2)

To set up **Affiliate tiers**, you must first click this **Activate** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F9Tbas7kpSvFgmpmFygqV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D129c2d97-5d0e-4dd2-aa71-9c8b0aa92cb3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d61f3eb7&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/motivate-affiliates/affiliate-tiers#example)

Example

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FNKVu0H6SNLwji0s8fwQz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43c69856-5cef-4842-bc90-3e24eb10916e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=548c0411&sv=2)

In this example, if affiliates reach $500 in sales, they will be automatically transferred from Program _Silver_ to Program _Gold_, which offers a higher commission rate.

# Default affiliate link | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

When an affiliate signs up for your program through BixGrow, a default affiliate link is automatically generated. This link is unique to each affiliate and is usually based on the main URL of your store, with a tracking parameter appended to it.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/default-affiliate-link#how-to-customize-default-affiliate-link)

How to customize default affiliate link?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, this link points to the homepage of your store. However, you can customize it so that all affiliate links direct to a specific product or collection page. This is especially useful if you want to focus your affiliate efforts on promoting particular products or categories.

You have two options to customize your affiliates’ default affiliate links:

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/default-affiliate-link#customize-default-affiliate-links-for-all-affiliates)

Customize default affiliate links for all affiliates

To update the default affiliate link for all affiliates in your program, kindly navigate to the **Settings** tab > **Affiliate Link** section and update the **Default Affiliate Link** field there.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F9809nl3cxXpElp3wxDHw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2cd4f4ec-8d7c-4588-a701-af50d90a45ae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7925b1cd&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/default-affiliate-link#customize-default-affiliate-link-for-each-affiliate-individually)

Customize default affiliate link for each affiliate individually

If you want to customize default affiliate link for individual affiliates, you can do so by going to the **Affiliates** tab, clicking on the name of the affiliate whose link you want to customize, and then customizing the link under the **Affiliate Link** section.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FHHHvnobAU2CHExAjNsGd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4009d02c-8cb4-42a4-9e9e-2f0bebb1edee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48f0988e&sv=2)

Then, fill in the **new redirect** you want for the default link (for example, a product's URL) and click **Save**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F5drU9Pdln00TwaRtAc2Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df22356b2-3742-470c-ab54-1200fc50644b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26f4a0c9&sv=2)

Now your affiliate has a new affiliate link that **redirects to a new URL**! You can also shorten it to your own liking or follow the affiliate's name to tell them out. If you want to keep the redirected URL the same and only rename the link, you can leave the **Enter a Home/Product/Collection URL** box empty and only click **Shorten link**.

Please keep in mind that Shopify now **only allows lower cases in redirects** (or shortened links here) so inserting upper cases to the shortened link will make the link redirect to an error 404 page instead of your destination page.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FQswSEDHkkY9OLfxaqDL2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4461f4e3-fd23-4a25-a4ea-2d7fe0fbc98a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50e6310b&sv=2)

This shortened affiliate link must **NOT be partially or completely the same** as the default affiliate link. For example, if the default affiliate link is _https://bixgrowtest.com/quinn?bg\_ref=3PF7VfZtzM_, do NOT create the custom affiliate link as _https://bixgrowtest.com/quinn_ or the two links will always redirect to each other in a never-ending loop, therefore causing an error!

[PreviousManage affiliate links](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links)
[NextProduct link](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/product-link)

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# How can affiliates share a coupon? | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-can-affiliates-share-a-coupon#how-can-affiliates-share-a-coupon)

How can affiliates share a coupon?

Affiliates can log in to the Affiliate Dashboard to retrieve their coupons. For Dynamic Coupons, affiliates only need to share their affiliate link with customers, and the coupon will be automatically generated when customers click the link.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F2r9ZBNvaqtAEf21FC9do%252FScreenshot_21.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5880bcf-d7b1-454d-ba27-70c599129f7e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f84b847&sv=2)

Affiliates have two options to share coupons:

*   **Share the affiliate link:** The coupon is automatically applied at checkout when customers make a purchase.
    
*   **Share the coupon code directly:** Customers manually enter the coupon at checkout.
    

When a customer makes a purchase using the coupon, they receive a discount, and the affiliate earns a commission.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-can-affiliates-share-a-coupon#auto-applied-coupon-at-checkout)

Auto-applied coupon at checkout

By default, **Dynamic Coupons** are always auto-applied at checkout when a customer clicks an affiliate link **(this cannot be turned off).**

For **Static Coupons**, you must **manually enable** the option "Auto-applied when customer uses affiliate link" when setting up the coupon.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FMzKjL9rlKI3eoa6Asyrb%252FScreenshot_3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9ef25f1-d8fd-49a3-8e39-44faafecd2da&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7559dee3&sv=2)

To disable this feature for Static Coupons, simply uncheck the “Auto-applied” box during coupon setup.

This setting allows you to control whether coupons are applied automatically or if customers need to enter them manually at checkout.

In case an affiliate has **multiple coupons**, **only the first one assigned** will be automatically applied when customers use their affiliate links.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-can-affiliates-share-a-coupon#example)

Example

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FdT3i6XPuNyhAguS1G18M%252FScreenshot_7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16a5f3dd-f860-463c-af33-a222dc1da043&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d908e206&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FOGo7KyRSnscWJQw10EsJ%252FScreenshot_9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c28e2c2-90e9-422e-afbc-8a5ab6573ec1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e99a0dec&sv=2)

[Previous How do affiliate coupons work?](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-do-affiliate-coupons-work)
[NextHow to generate & assign coupons to affiliates?](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-to-generate-and-assign-coupons-to-affiliates)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Static coupon | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Go to Programs > Edit program > Customer Discount and select Static Coupon under the Discount type section.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FeapMxegemuLvzQzak5Oj%252FScreenshot_26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b6b1deb-1c0e-4e72-819b-a502cfe50c14&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=63398840&sv=2)

The coupon is **automatically assigned** to each affiliate after being approved to join your program. This type of coupon is **fixed, reusable, and shareable**.

If “Auto-applied” is enabled, the coupon will be automatically applied at checkout when a customer visits the store through the affiliate's link. You can also choose to allow affiliates to customize their coupon name if desired.

[PreviousManage coupons](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/manage-coupons)
[NextDynamic Coupon](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/manage-coupons/dynamic-coupon)

Last updated 4 months ago

# How to generate & assign coupons to affiliates? | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-to-generate-and-assign-coupons-to-affiliates#id-1.-auto-generated-coupons-customer-discount-recommended)

**1\. Auto-generated Coupons/Customer Discount (👉 recommended)**

With this method, merchants can automatically assign coupons to all affiliates within a program, making it easy to manage and ensuring consistency. It saves time, reduces manual effort, and ensures all affiliates within the program receive their coupons efficiently.

There are two types of coupons: Static Coupons, which are fixed and sharable, and Dynamic Coupons, which are automatically generated after clicking affiliate links.

[**Learn more about the difference between Static coupons & Dynamic coupons**](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/affiliate-coupon#affiliate-coupon-types)

Go to Programs > Edit program > Customer Discount

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FOS6AWOzZv6yUye9mQK0X%252FScreenshot_11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D734338f7-3a8c-4b84-adec-68b23803c2ac&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f831865a&sv=2)

After a coupon is created, a coupon template will be generated in the Coupons tab for easy management. You can edit this template, and all coupons under that template will be updated accordingly.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F3Bzj4TRaNsOHywxZcoId%252FScreenshot_23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63c1763b-e8e3-4c18-8dde-16308daaf984&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=75e3f6fd&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-to-generate-and-assign-coupons-to-affiliates#id-2.-single-assign)

2\. Single Assign

Merchants can manually assign a coupon to a specific affiliate. This method is useful for personalizing offers, testing different strategies, or providing exclusive discounts to selected affiliates.

Go to Coupons > Codes > Assign coupon

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F24tQX8D6GrZBrkbndeUE%252FScreenshot_28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea7f83ae-ed50-4f31-9f8b-24ab9ea4e92d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2299d5a0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FYQgd9yWMr9HNbsdKpD2D%252FScreenshot_13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00ffc244-7306-4601-bf2d-0573a415b579&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3be9d048&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-to-generate-and-assign-coupons-to-affiliates#id-3.-bulk-assign)

3\. Bulk Assign

This method allows merchants to assign coupons to multiple affiliates at once, which is ideal for seasonal promotions or large-scale campaigns. It streamlines the process and ensures multiple affiliates receive their codes simultaneously without manual effort.

Go to Coupons > Codes > Assign coupon

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FY20Bm2tHrxWN7zEh40YW%252FScreenshot_29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D015f3c54-cd67-4a26-9311-0a006e936473&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=680e6ca9&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FRDAkDZU8T7SXm0CJMhx7%252FScreenshot_15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7ec20fd-4468-4387-bf8a-628f6d14d31b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef1595d0&sv=2)

Once the coupons are bulk-assigned, a coupon template will also be created in the Coupons tab. This allows you to easily edit the template later, and the changes will apply to all coupons within that template.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FSLelb84SyP8XXp4Rdbqj%252FScreenshot_24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9032dac2-d761-47cb-9b59-ace0e17be49e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e98c9732&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-to-generate-and-assign-coupons-to-affiliates#id-4.-bulk-import)

4\. Bulk Import

You can bulk import existing affiliate coupons into your programs. This is extremely useful when you migrate from another app.

This feature is **enabled upon request for eligible users only**. We require a legit affiliate coupon list and a subscription to a paid plan.

To do so, you must first contact us to enable the **Import** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F9pLI8hcjraB2CNUz9lEt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D467d9913-bb53-4679-a49a-95401a6e7ab9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1da54b3d&sv=2)

1.  Upload your CSV file (_email_ and _coupon_ columns are required)
    
2.  Click **Import coupons**
    

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F3vlY5Bhm2JprDfcos7bI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D939a07ed-99c3-4ff3-80cb-ea5755611ed5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ff5c6d00&sv=2)

**Download our sample CSV file** to set up your data field columns correctly!

[PreviousHow can affiliates share a coupon?](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-can-affiliates-share-a-coupon)
[NextManage coupons](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/manage-coupons)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Automated Shopify tags for referral orders | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Here, you can include **Order tags** that automatically apply to all referral orders in Shopify and help you tell them out from non-referral orders.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fex5GVpMwb3hs3jVIJlq8%252FScreenshot_21.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deaa25149-6c92-497f-bbcd-6e14296f5451&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d774669&sv=2)

You can set the order tag format with different variables: {full\_name}, {email}, {phone}, {company}, {commission}, {username}.

[PreviousAuto-adjustments for returns and refunded orders](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/adjustments-for-returns-and-refunds)

# Registration fees | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

This is where you can require affiliates to pay membership fees for joining your programs. Affiliates will then sign up, pay the fee, and be accepted into the program once the payment has been confirmed.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/registration-fees#id-1.-activate-your-paypal-recipient-account)

1\. Activate your PayPal recipient account

First, please bind the PayPal account that you're going to use for receiving membership fees from affiliates. Before we begin, please remember that a **PayPal Business Account** is required for activation.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/registration-fees#log-in-to-your-paypal-account)

Log in to [your PayPal account](https://www.paypal.com/)

Log in using your **PayPal** account's email address and password.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fzsbc0M0MjK6tNpD2TFEQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd692622-b174-4e3d-ac56-e2545e63b484&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b92df9a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FGZ1LTuAhjqxIWk5K2432%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debc6c5a2-d94a-447e-ab5a-7bcb3c6e66b5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0303d26&sv=2)

Here, click on **Developer** to access your **PayPal Developer Dashboard**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FUdAb7JXyFzhlbVnPWmKr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D237da28d-b432-466a-8be4-9937717af2fb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0d879ac&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F1toEyFpdgrWyNhIqH2Yt%252FScreenshot_9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6545708a-2635-43e7-9d8d-b05659c452c5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef8c47d5&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/registration-fees#create-your-app)

Create your app

Go to **Apps & Credentials,** switch from **Sandbox** to **Live** mode, and then click **Create App**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F7VCmVI2JUyhi9PbVdU4C%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5968e61c&sv=2)

Keep in mind that you MUST switch to **Live** mode. If you don't, the credentials attained from the app you create will be deemed **invalid**.

Next, fill in the app name (e.g. **BixGrow Membership**) and click **Create App**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FFr9Zzlmcw9kEHgFRUJDD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33260171-0c6b-40fa-8d43-168790baee83&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5df40151&sv=2)

Now, you will see your **Client ID** and **Secret**, which will be used in the next step.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FDKHFFuXgP46jD8KeyrAe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9b38e43-15aa-4640-8688-acf626aed70d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=23f710f9&sv=2)

(optional) You can scroll down and uncheck the **Payouts** box, as there's no need for this feature to receive payments.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FbRZduUQqc7ClnwnFcNGf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1f47407-0ce0-4d55-8148-d535d0174fb5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b21913d6&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/registration-fees#activate-in-bixgrow)

Activate in BixGrow

Return to **BixGrow** \> **Extra functions** \> **Membership Fees** and click the **Activate** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FZvHK38AkS0L21eqJRE5j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3dc5bb8-811b-4765-a15e-c562e9151e8e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a7d5cea4&sv=2)

Then, enter the **Client ID** and **Secret key** you just got from PayPal.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FIN6GvB8LNQLOl5xOY80Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b4326b5-5acb-49c3-9f9b-64a89b16eb22&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5345f2b4&sv=2)

Finally, click **Save**. You can now start creating **membership plans**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F9OGsjRBpSumgJvewCttI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da886f198-d562-4423-b132-9d8106f27ac7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a1173c6&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/registration-fees#id-2.-create-membership-plans)

2\. Create membership plans

Please click on this **New payment plan** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FXIMf9cvncbNL9bY6O9Id%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4d35b22-25c9-41e0-a6d0-65d9d3216124&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ce30c6aa&sv=2)

Here you can put a name to the plan, select the program to which this plan will apply, set up the fee amount, and describe which perks are included when affiliates join this program with a membership.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FD7K1Qz3y8sp7Sfyw4960%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a6cf3b0-a6e1-4def-a174-8c1eb3a1aa7d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a922d396&sv=2)

Save the change once you're done. Now you can see that the **membership plan** is live and ready for any affiliate who signs up for this program.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FCOONYeOg2YI4rhAiGMbn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D694c291a-96eb-4658-b105-b9f967550183&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fbfe8175&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/registration-fees#example)

Example

Here I sign up for the _Membership Plan Test_ program - which I created a **membership plan** for.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FubaJl6ySIAWs0e05ZZFD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5e98a2f-e728-40dd-b360-204a668d058d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0be91ee&sv=2)

I submit my registration and am redirected to this page, where I can pay my membership fee.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FlVmuoxOzCwuvgec2RQiE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc35cef70-c42b-4807-b579-9387c66710ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b47f5eed&sv=2)

I'm redirected to PayPal to finish my payment. Once I finish, I'm redirected back to the affiliate dashboard of the program I signed up for, now already logged in.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FAY5HlET0cjGjySPLqi14%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfbaf9a98-ddde-4a94-8a83-832844fd6262&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=704dee90&sv=2)

The approval setting of an affiliate program stays the same with **Membership Plans** - just an extra registration fee required. If the program is set to auto-approve affiliates (as in my example), affiliates will be redirected to the affiliate dashboard right after finishing payment, already logged in. If the program is not set to auto-approve affiliates, they will have to wait for the merchant's decision normally.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/registration-fees#id-3.-review-membership-plans)

3\. Review membership plans

You can click on **Re-configure** if you'd like to use another PayPal account to receive membership payments.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F54C5dj6qyR9jnBh1LNW9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e834988-f9e0-4cca-a935-fa4c51a804e3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6c9b8f45&sv=2)

Or on **Subscription History** to get a complete overview of affiliates who finished their membership payments.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FtPNdFYJ0B2IevWE9ITTP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D891e6703-71be-457e-8eab-b6315155f138&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b1c2ed&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F6uaH0JGwUw4fOKfmtHIT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2e867f6-c41c-4f25-9306-e905301fd71f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=11a55c2a&sv=2)

If you no longer want to charge a registration fee for a program, please delete its payment plan here.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FW5hpAuRdwLBJBS2BiOlo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5880816b-1b6c-4123-a207-d396b03ac35c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=120dcd54&sv=2)

# Custom link | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Affiliates have the option to create custom links directly from their dashboard. They can select specific page in your store, add their own tracking parameters, and even shorten these links if needed. This customization helps affiliates to better target their audience and track the effectiveness of their campaigns.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/custom-link#how-to-create-a-custom-link)

How to create a Custom Link?

Let’s say an affiliate only wants to promote Product A. While the **Product Links** page in the dashboard displays the entire product list, the **Custom Link** feature allows the affiliate to create a link directly to Product A (or any specific product or collection page) without having to sift through a long list of products.

To promote Product A, affiliate can log in to their Affiliate Dashboard, find the **Custom Link** page and then click **Create now.**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F7QhQ4ZRg43zkiXslrRbn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29abdf89-85fc-4bcd-b2cd-b350e96c189a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95b3f98c&sv=2)

Now copy and paste the URL of the specific product or collection page from merchant's store into the field.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FvOgOs5hBY6CjmkHruHWH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D977c1da9-77ea-4169-9d85-5654b2de22f1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b7f45b8f&sv=2)

After clicking **Create**, the link will be shown in the list under the Custom Links tab for the affiliate to copy and use at any time.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FYzCz74mpp03epMbgIw9D%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e7c5028-7361-47ee-b60d-c3f3dcd5ed5c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26a9fe70&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/custom-link#using-shortened-links)

Using Shortened Links

If the affiliate prefers a cleaner, shorter link for sharing (for instance, on social media), they can use the **Shortened Link** option. After generating the custom affiliate link, they can click the option to shorten it, making it easier to share while still maintaining full tracking functionality.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FhWlsMPLEGqslHSlK5Jge%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D909dd353-4481-4efd-8b35-6f646b3d69f4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=efc4e476&sv=2)

Affiliates can customize the shortened link field by filling in a name or keyword that makes the link easier to share and recognizable for customers.

For example, in the screenshot below:

*   The default product link is: [https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/products/sponge-chocolate-cake](https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/products/sponge-chocolate-cake)
    
*   The generated affiliate link is: [https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/products/sponge-chocolate-cake?bg\_ref=VQ9q75ODfg&utm\_source=aff](https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/products/sponge-chocolate-cake?bg_ref=VQ9q75ODfg&utm_source=aff)
    
*   The shortened affiliate link is: [https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/Evelyn](https://bixgrow-demo-store.myshopify.com/Evelyn)
    

As you can see, the new shortened link is shorter, more organized, and easier to share.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FLFnWYekCQ0XQbHtaB4Co%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11e95741-4e1e-4f97-8e87-ed7d5db1d684&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b1eacdf&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/custom-link#how-can-affiliates-track-their-traffic)

How can affiliates track their traffic?

Once an affiliate has created their custom link, they may want to track where their traffic is coming from, such as clicks from social media platforms like Facebook, Instagram, ect. The app allows affiliates to add tracking parameters to their custom links, making it easier to monitor the performance of their campaigns from different sources.

Let’s say the affiliate wants to share their custom link on _Instagram_, where it’s being used in an _ad_ for _Campaign No. 1_. They want to track the traffic and conversions coming from this specific campaign. They can do this by adding a custom tracking parameter to the link, as shown in the screenshot below.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FfHL8TretYkfcXSV9VcwZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6615371b-aa56-41ad-841a-f649f7114d4c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a002fc5a&sv=2)

This way, affiliates can create multiple custom links with different tracking parameters for more precise tracking purposes.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/custom-link#creating-custom-links-on-merchants-side)

Creating Custom Links on merchant's side

Merchants can also log in to the affiliate dashboard to help creating custom affiliate links.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F7pfIfCz6XW71k6TLP3EL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba9382b3-127c-4b12-97a7-bb2367f68130&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a2ae4778&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/custom-link#enabling-custom-links-for-affiliates)

**Enabling Custom Links for Affiliates**

Merchants can choose whether to allow affiliates to customize their affiliate links. To enable this feature, kindly go to **Settings** > **Affiliate Link** and then toggle on the **Allow Affiliates to Custom Link** option.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FnV20Cq8frvGW9c4SeRxb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9385e8e2-c9e7-4461-aef1-e232d69648d5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6395d942&sv=2)

If you decide not to allow affiliates to create custom links, simply leave this feature disabled.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/custom-link#hiding-the-custom-link-section)

Hiding the Custom Link Section

If you prefer, you can hide the custom link section from the Affiliate Dashboard. This might be useful if you want to keep the process simple for affiliates or if you want to maintain control over the links being used. To do this kindly go to **Settings** \> **Affiliate portal** > **Customize Affiliate Dashboard** and then click on the eye icon next to the **Custom Links** section.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fzf33sJaowsQNzLblPRyO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1700f004-7e87-4f3c-b2f6-60efcc2ad102&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f437fa3b&sv=2)

[PreviousProduct link](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/product-link)
[NextAuto-shortened link](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/auto-shortened-link)

# Auto-adjustments for returns and refunded orders | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Suppose you give a referral order a refund by selecting item(s) in the order. In that case, **BixGrow** will reverse the previous commission calculations and deduct commissions based on the product(s) refunded. If only some selected items in the order were refunded and not all, the affiliate will still receive a partial commission. If all items in the order were refunded, the affiliate will not receive any commission for that order at all.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/adjustments-for-returns-and-refunds#example)

Example

This is a referral order of 4 items and how it was recorded, displayed, and explained in BixGrow.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fui0us1pi74rdoTVU5tqW%252FScreenshot_72.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D580662eb-943b-4ab7-9d91-c67ad4d7a452&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7d32a669&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F0SvzSehu7pT9QBiiyqzQ%252FScreenshot_73.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff7fac76-dee4-437c-a111-237531012021&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e4fa0d9&sv=2)

How it was auto-adjusted when 2 items are selected to be refunded on Shopify:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FMWXKDr6PDWySIScC1ROW%252FScreenshot_74.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2bf50a9b-d5cf-408c-88ae-30a4b1ec89e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3169d0a3&sv=2)

As paid commissions can't be deducted even if the original order was refunded, it's recommended to pay your affiliates not immediately but only **after the return time limit** specified in your store's Return Policy (for example, after 15 days from the order was placed). Also, please **select items** from the order you need to refund instead of paying a custom amount of refund.

[PreviousHow conversions are tracked](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/how-conversions-are-tracked)
[NextAutomated Shopify tags for referral orders](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/automated-shopify-tags-for-referral-orders)

# How conversions are tracked | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

This is where you can keep track of what affiliates bring back to your shop, including **Commissions**, **Clicks**, and **Customers**.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/how-conversions-are-tracked#id-1.-commissions)

1\. Commissions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A **commission** is calculated when an order is recorded to be placed via an **affiliate link** (directly/indirectly but during the time period of **cookie duration**) or using an affiliate **coupon** at checkout. The order also had to be **marked as paid** on Shopify. There are the order's date, order number, the affiliate who brought the order, order's total sale, commission amount, commission status, payment status, order's tracking method and actions (approve/deny/view commission details).

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F7MF5uVuiKi4j7lKMhTkX%252FScreenshot_63.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45be2643-ca19-44a6-8de2-e71a56bcbed8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d7f84ea&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/how-conversions-are-tracked#id-2.-clicks)

2\. Clicks


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is where you can see the list of **clicks** on all affiliate links. There are the click's date, insights (customer's used device, browser and OS), the affiliate whose link was clicked, referrer URL (if the link was clicked on another site and not directly accessed - for example, Facebook), and destination URL which is the exact link that was clicked.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fmnwg09NJPl2dOpEwW1fV%252FScreenshot_64.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df30de251-9294-41d6-8e65-3a7be2078e1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1122a796&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/how-conversions-are-tracked#id-3.-customers)

3\. Customers

This is where you can see the list of **customers** brought by all affiliates.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F309NAJqLrguvfn53zagr%252FScreenshot_65.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a8507a7-72a3-4b28-865b-f84cae33698b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36c9b624&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/how-conversions-are-tracked#id-4.-when-are-conversions-tracked)

4\. When are conversions tracked?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Referral orders having the payment status as **Paid** will appear automatically in **BixGrow** without waiting until fulfillment. Our app doesn't track Unpaid orders.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/how-conversions-are-tracked#id-5.-how-does-the-tracking-pending-referral-orders-feature-work-and-should-it-be-enabled)

5\. How does the Tracking pending referral orders feature work and should it be enabled?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This feature allows you to monitor orders that are pending processing. Depending on your demand, you can decide whether to enable this feature or not. If you want full control over the tracking process of orders, enabling this feature can be useful to ensure you always have a comprehensive view of referral orders.

You must go to **Settings** \> **Advanced**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FBFEDGjpPxhNKClSUGO2v%252FScreenshot_29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb53d916-68d4-420a-b4eb-590b84809e77&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4b17d58&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/how-conversions-are-tracked#id-6.-why-are-orders-not-tracked-why-have-orders-not-been-tracked-yet)

6\. Why are orders not tracked/ Why have orders not been tracked yet?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are several reasons why an order may not be tracked:

\- Customers didn’t place orders via an **affiliate link** or use an **affiliate coupon** at checkout

\- Customers placed orders via an affiliate link but the **Tracking by link** feature was turned off

\- Customers checked out using a third-party payment gateway (not Shopify Payments)

\- The order hasn’t been **paid**/**marked as paid** on Shopify yet

\- An advanced commission rule that **disables tracking** orders placed by **existing customers**

\- Orders containing discount codes are set to **No tracking**

[PreviousAdd/Approve/Deny/Import a conversion](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/add-approve-deny-a-conversion)
[NextAuto-adjustments for returns and refunded orders](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/adjustments-for-returns-and-refunds)

Last updated 1 year ago

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/add-payment-methods/how-to-add-payment-methods#q1.-why-cant-my-affiliates-choose-any-payment-methods)

**Q1. Why can't my affiliates choose any payment methods?**

A1. You haven't offered affiliates any payment methods to choose from yet.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/add-payment-methods/how-to-add-payment-methods#q2.-how-can-i-add-different-payment-methods-for-each-program)

**Q2. How can I add different payment methods for each program?**

A2. By default, the payment methods you selected are common for all programs. However, you can reach out to **our Support team** to have the different payment method settings for each program option enabled!

# Prevent affiliate commissions for self-purchases | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Our **Fraud protection** feature ensures the integrity of your affiliate program by preventing affiliates from earning commissions on their self-purchases.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FxE6VEvjDnDaNGHzWfUs8%252FScreenshot_20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2cf8b66-ad67-453b-a59b-c4707d5ca9de&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4247c291&sv=2)

We offer three types of **Fraud protection**:

1.  **Same affiliate and Customer email address:** Affiliates will not receive commissions if their email address matches that of the customer.
    
2.  **Same affiliate and Customer IP address:** Affiliates will not receive commissions if their IP address matches that of the customer. (An IP address is a unique identifier assigned to a device, and matching IP addresses likely indicate the use of the same device.)
    
3.  **Same affiliate and Customer first and last name:** Affiliates will not receive commissions if their first and last names match those of the customer.
    

[PreviousAutomated Shopify tags for referral orders](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/automated-shopify-tags-for-referral-orders)
[NextReports](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/reports)

Last updated 1 year ago

# How to make payments: A-Z | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Here you'll find a list of commission payouts for you to base on and pay your affiliates. For each commission amount, we offer all the information you need to make payments including the payment amounts, payment methods selected by affiliates, and maybe a **Pay** button depending on the said payment methods.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z#step-1-generate-a-payout)

Step 1: Generate a payout

You'll first need to click the **Generate payout** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FEf82uAFQ6KfixHl5Ev5C%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dabfcc9d0-c1b0-4ea2-8988-b3a078d8b217&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d6d8bd7&sv=2)

You can generate a payout for all approved orders so far or until a specific date only. **You can also use filters to find payouts you need** to make: program, affiliate, minimum amount, and payment method.

This is how it looks when a payout is successfully generated:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FALxObHnHmQQdgoMrzlDK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83d9f4b0-da53-4765-af45-c7f01f6c3db1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=261131a7&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z#step-2-review-the-payout)

Step 2: Review the payout

You can click the payout just created and check to make sure the commission amount and all payment info were generated correctly.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FhVQfwTXjsWn5hsNlOrzr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d9a8b9a-b0a8-4e07-943c-6ffa295532a2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eb891687&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z#step-3-pay-affiliates)

**Step 3: Pay affiliates**

Based on the payout generated and reviewed, you can proceed to pay your affiliates using the payment methods they selected: **Manual payment** or **In-app payment**.

Once all 3 steps are completed, the payout's billing status in BixGrow will change from **Unpaid** to **Paid** and our system will send the affiliate an **email notification** of the payout.

# Product link | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Affiliates can obtain links for every product by navigating to their **Affiliate Dashboard** > **Product Links** tab.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FIEk3Nh8KyzBDbF19AOId%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55ef41fb-6651-40c5-ab1f-312d04e62c26&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e48d66f8&sv=2)

There they have two options to choose from:

**Standard Link**: The full, original link that includes the product URL and tracking parameters.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FO7PHeNgUMqUiav4GpMZc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3203b40a-4dc2-4323-9483-781e7cc981e1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b70f7d16&sv=2)

**Shortened Link**: A more concise version of the product link, making it easier to share on social media and other platforms.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FIE1FPlHWfQMP8YZG3UZZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e342abf-ef86-4db7-ad14-6779b1881d65&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9c2da0c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/product-link#hiding-the-product-link-section)

Hiding the Product Link Section

If you prefer that your affiliates only promote using the default affiliate link, you have the option to hide the **Product Links** page from their dashboard. To do this kindly go to **Settings** > **Affiliate portal** > **Customize Affiliate Dashboard > Data visibility** and then click on the eye icon next to the **Product Links** section.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F3GZQboMru0L4NPy02GGh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dddb54e42-7480-4d78-ac16-19db92c64b92&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b18872ba&sv=2)

This will remove the Product Links page from the affiliate dashboard, ensuring that affiliates focus on using the default link you’ve set up.

#  How do affiliate coupons work? | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-do-affiliate-coupons-work#how-do-affiliate-coupons-work)

How do affiliate coupons work?

Affiliate Coupons allow store owners to provide affiliates with unique discount codes that their referred customers can use when making purchases. This feature helps incentivize customers while also tracking affiliate performance effectively.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FvZoQD1O2L9xprZsm4bwH%252Faf-tracking-method-coupon.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc43ab977-ae9b-4acb-848e-9f6641131587&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1cf84fed&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-do-affiliate-coupons-work#faq)

FAQ

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-do-affiliate-coupons-work#id-1.-how-to-know-if-an-order-is-tracked-by-a-coupon-or-link)

1\. How to know if an order is tracked by a coupon or link?

To check if an order is attributed to a coupon or affiliate link, go to the Conversions tab in the BixGrow app.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-do-affiliate-coupons-work#id-2.-can-an-affiliate-have-multiple-coupon-codes)

2\. Can an affiliate have multiple coupon codes?

Yes, a single affiliate can be assigned multiple coupon codes. This allows them to use different codes for different campaigns or target audiences.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-do-affiliate-coupons-work#id-3.-if-an-affiliate-has-more-than-one-coupon-which-one-will-be-auto-applied-when-customers-purchase-v)

3\. If an affiliate has more than one coupon, which one will be auto-applied when customers purchase via affiliate links?

In this situation, the first assigned coupon will be auto-applied at checkout.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-do-affiliate-coupons-work#id-4.-is-it-possible-to-allow-customers-to-use-many-coupons-on-an-order)

4\. Is it possible to allow customers to use many coupons on an order?

By choosing the Combinations while setting up affiliate coupons, customers will be able to use more than one coupon on an order.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-do-affiliate-coupons-work#id-5.-if-a-customer-applies-an-affiliate-coupon-at-checkout-manually-without-accessing-via-an-affiliate)

**5\. If a customer applies an affiliate coupon at checkout manually (without accessing via an affiliate link), can the affiliate earn a commission?**

Yes, affiliates can earn commissions if customers purchase using affiliate coupons or affiliate links. It is not compulsory to use both of them at the same time.

[PreviousAdd UTM to affiliate links](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/add-utm-to-affiliate-links)
[NextHow can affiliates share a coupon?](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-can-affiliates-share-a-coupon)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Dynamic Coupon | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Go to Programs > Edit program > Customer Discount and select Dynamic Coupon under the Discount type section.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F4Wjy9ela8dp4cMNTvh7G%252FScreenshot_25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e04536b-d313-498b-bb4c-9e2f74d4b742&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1dfed01&sv=2)

This type of coupon is a **one-time-use discount code**, being generated **only when a customer clicks an affiliate link**.

Unlike Static Coupons, Dynamic Coupons are automatically applied at checkout by default when a customer purchases via an affiliate link (no need to enable the “Auto-applied” option). Additionally, affiliates cannot edit their dynamic coupon name, as each code is uniquely generated for each customer.

To fully activate and display the dynamic coupon, make sure the **Discount popup** is enabled in Settings > Onsite-Content > Discount popup.

The Discount popup appears when a visitor clicks an affiliate link and highlights:

*   The affiliate’s name
    
*   The discount details
    
*   A copyable coupon code
    

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FeBYeFXJSt9NDUYmL8If6%252FScreenshot_27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D834b0468-7f35-49a5-b7f8-b280d9c7bb71&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fb890e4e&sv=2)

[PreviousStatic coupon](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/manage-coupons/static-coupon)
[NextAdd/Approve/Deny/Import a conversion](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/add-approve-deny-a-conversion)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Log in to an Affiliate dashboard | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

As a merchant, you can log in as your affiliates to view their dashboards and check if all settings and displays are alright. To do so, you just first click this **Log in as affiliate** button on the affiliate profiles.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FQtnpep3gFfBvQUfc92YG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0f5df44-cc71-4ed1-9591-0eb45bcf27bd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=104f0392&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#id-1.-dashboard)

**1\.** Dashboard


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In **Affiliate dashboard,** you can view the affiliate's performance including clicks, orders, total sales, and commissions in detailed status. Affiliate links (default and custom), coupons, and bonuses that the affiliate is eligible to earn are also displayed.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F2EpQZK8GF7HelvPxpzRT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7ca62a7-d20b-47fd-b676-021639fddd03&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=321be69d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#id-2.-links-and-assets)

2\. Links & Assets


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#a.-custom-links)

**a. Custom links**

This is where affiliates can customize their own default links by adding tracking parameters (UTMs) or renaming them. To create a custom affiliate link, you must first click this **Create now** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fypv7jKGS3YyIksUg42yr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe9da1cc-38fd-4346-becd-8d409908dc54&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e68e5087&sv=2)

Then enable **Add tracking parameters** box if you need it for further tracking purposes (for example, Google Analytics). 3 tracking IDs can be added max to find out which channels are more effective for the affiliate to promote. You can also click **Shorten link** to tell the sources.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FAsuat00UtHm7JskfxOoE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4eb031f4-b426-4a99-82e4-62f4ff3f91d2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a3ecf65&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F9GVwBX2RNUFJmcmlgNjL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8114113d-dc22-49ee-8fcd-6a8abad14bf6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=524ee977&sv=2)

Now click **Create** and your affiliate will have a new affiliate link that **has tracking parameters added**. These IDs are then viewable in **Clicks** for you to see the original channels that the clicks came from after you enabled tracking IDs' columns.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FuEGwMqb8ryx2f2GcLQ8p%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5d40da7-0f47-47ad-ac4e-3d67f0f0f33d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db235482&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FIZ2WOnH7W8hLfCMu5BT1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D18943473-d831-4391-b0b1-7f7800f2d9ac&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b6458049&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#b.-product-links)

**b. Product Links**

Normally, a default affiliate link directs to your store, so this feature is extremely useful when you want to get an affiliate link for a specific product/collection page without having to leave the app.

To create a product link as an affiliate, you must first click the **Get link** button on the desired product/collection card.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F45hICOwtt4aLhBJIG6BJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52f7f114-d1dd-477c-b47b-3961a18fd22b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f86ae3c7&sv=2)

You can also get a shortened link for better promotion!

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F6xTbKlirrYjgvUHDwb5G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D405dbbbc-a057-437d-bdf5-a94555a27b12&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1a91fa4f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#c.-coupons)

**c. Coupons**

This is where affiliates can view (and edit if allowed) their coupon codes.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FaLfrllEVzUrID3MO1Fqc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df45c4422-70b8-4f26-a02f-db02a1026289&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=648ea5ea&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#d.-media)

**d. Media**

Here all the marketing assets that you uploaded to help affiliates promote in the **Creatives** tab of your own dashboard can be viewed and used.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FbmXvrGPM8LUcHE8Oh3Ey%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df166edcf-6d7f-4fe1-976c-b5cb43ac9f1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2a98856a&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#id-3.-commissions)

**3\. Commissions**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In **Conversions**, you can see commissions, clicks, and customers brought by the affiliate. Please keep in mind that affiliates can **only view** the commissions and explanations, they are **unable** to review or change the commissions' status.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fzi1orjzF5s3rvxYtETtt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fba5761-bda6-4db0-aa00-0ac42987c6ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba6b1ea0&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#id-4.-clicks)

4\. Clicks


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In **Clicks**, you can view insights into the clicks on the affiliate's link.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fw2a4ahKfYzUvbKd4czsl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2ee9ea5-902c-4667-b57e-75a06b323175&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3353429f&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#id-5.-payouts)

5\. Payouts


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In **Payouts**, you can see a list of payments that you paid the affiliate and their explanation.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F19scrfoF0uAUX5QNfNUX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a143b03-fd16-4111-9f62-4c7725f5c293&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d17af430&sv=2)

If your affiliate selected **Store credit** as a payment method, then in the **Store credit** tab, they can see their generated coupons and generate new ones by themselves if allowed **here**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FNnafWrfdp8YJqDoqq7jP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a12b482-be97-4f18-88f2-c32fbcc78d4c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d19b1b8&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#id-6.-network)

6\. Network


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In **Network**, the affiliate's network link (to invite more affiliates/downlines into the program) and total network commission can be viewed, along with their network commission history and affiliate tree.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fr3TE32jsM15BvSfpTwap%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D868fd531-f6d4-4cb5-9f5f-b33fff5cb902&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=291bbdf9&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#id-7.-reports)

7\. Reports


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is where the affiliate can view detailed **reports** of their performances including total **clicks**, **orders**, **sales** they brought back, and their total earned **commissions**. You can filter the results by time range and parameters.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fztr8XcHKlTUBLJdTK9ec%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f2b0174-143f-42bc-91aa-c41daee6f756&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef2b7f85&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#id-8.-program-directory)

**8\. Program directory**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a complete summary of what all affiliates need to know about their affiliate programs.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FDX0PSjow3tXcCrIQWgX5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97003bb9-9dcf-49bb-8826-08071263ed26&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=350ad15f&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/log-in-to-an-affiliate-dashboard#id-9.-profile)

9\. Profile


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In **Profile**, the affiliate's profile information can be added or edited.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F1TYrce8J1vOX1z4xvBYS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfee6c596-3533-4b54-9a50-e7f272fd9c9b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36f0b0cd&sv=2)

Plus, **Payment method** and **Sign-in credentials** can be set up or changed here.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F8BjVa89ACq1mPe6qGpyl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D379a0305-501a-441b-b03a-78d57d2f09f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c4da2d7&sv=2)

# Add UTM to affiliate links | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

To set up this feature, navigate to **Settings** > **Affiliate** **link** and click **Set up** button in the **Add UTM to affiliate links** section.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FibOTJUMTBpBCYrrvkKAq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5eadee18-556f-41f6-8bbc-70af3fd0e873&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=79cf6467&sv=2)

Simply input your desired parameters, and the app automatically generates a ready-to-use affiliate link with UTM tags. This way, you can measure the success of your campaigns and make data-driven decisions to boost your affiliate marketing strategy.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FVdLQAKfquzCEVjVn0w8D%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D663ec499-742e-48cf-b981-9ddea38da38a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8dcb3e16&sv=2)

BixGrow provides three customizable UTM tracking fields to help you track and analyze affiliate traffic effectively:

*   **Campaign Source**: This field identifies your affiliates. We recommend using the variables `{affiliate_name}`, `{affiliate_email}`, or `{referral_code}`, as these are unique to each affiliate.
    
*   **Campaign Medium**: Use this field to specify the type of traffic. Common examples are "affiliate" or "partner."
    
*   **Campaign Name**: This field is typically used to identify your program. We recommend using the variable `{program_name}`, or you can enter a specific campaign name to differentiate it from other campaigns in your store.
    

Once saved, a standard affiliate link with UTM parameters will look like this:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FRZ6H2JCKyCt2B3yM5a2s%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff7f93f8-30a8-4569-8709-2ef554f7eff8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=188a4b4d&sv=2)

You can edit or delete this setup at any time by clicking the pen icon or the three dots next to the example link.

After setting up UTM tracking, here’s how a default affiliate link will look. You also have the option to [shorten](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/manage-affiliate-links/auto-shortened-link)
 it, making the link cleaner and more professional for affiliates to share.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FhSDCcplLKJrvcu7iGLvK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad577317-47e0-4cd4-8e98-3312308f6446&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=47d65b27&sv=2)

From your UTM link setup in BixGrow, you can connect to your **Google Analytics** account to access detailed statistics about traffic generated by affiliate links. In Google Analytics, you can also filter the data based on **Source**, **Medium**, or **Campaign**, allowing you to compare performance and gain deeper insights into your affiliate program's effectiveness.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FFNWjUxcwH8aXMaxLARYJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D597d5dc8-a0ec-42b1-8526-61ad53883686&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a1179b47&sv=2)

[PreviousTrack affiliate link clicks](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-links/track-affiliate-link-clicks)
[Next How do affiliate coupons work?](https://docs.bixgrow.com/coupons/how-do-affiliate-coupons-work)

Last updated 10 months ago

# Customize sign-up page | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

To customize the **Sign-up page**, you must navigate to **Settings** > **Affiliate portal** > **Sign-up page** > **Customize**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FS5oPLQ4vsMdunUqMO2dg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7ab707a-fa3d-44bd-bd81-dedfd1ad2a47&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ae560c7d&sv=2)

Since each program can have a different sign-up page, you will first need to select a program! You can also choose to preview the page on a desktop or mobile device (you can hide the background image in mobile view).

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FZmiy3mykOwu2lOUeAbVI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb64b4d6-4109-4660-beeb-c93bb7c0b0f2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13a43579&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliates/use-the-sign-up-page/edit#edit-section)

Edit section


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is where you can customize and select which elements to display in the sign-up form.

This is where you can customize and choose which elements are to be displayed in the sign-up form (by clicking the **Eye** **icon**).

You are free to edit, delete any sample elements or add more, redesign, or reposition.

# VAT & Tax | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

This is where you can decide if affiliates' personal income tax is included in the payout calculation, and who should pay it. If in your country, your affiliates don't have an obligation to pay one for the commissions they earned from you, you just have to leave this section as its default - "None".

For example, the tax amount your affiliates have to pay is 5%, so you fill in 5% here. Now you're the one who pays them extra so that they can cover the tax part. Affiliate A earns a $10 commission from a $100 order she brought you, and as you're the tax payer, you'll be paying her $10 (commission) + $5 (tax) in total for that order, so that she can use the extra $5 to pay her tax later.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fps6jr5zuJjYxmpsbDe3t%252FScreenshot_48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D40fdba4f-8712-4f64-9303-4abe21f1797a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=df1bcfd3&sv=2)

This is an example of a payout with a 5% personal income tax included.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F1Eo4KQBDQYlz72RLlD3A%252FScreenshot_49.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcfaea4b6-73cc-41e8-b66d-bdfe0cacf2f3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c0fcd7f&sv=2)

Likewise, if you select **Affiliates** as the tax payer, they'll have to take the said amount from their commissions and pay by themselves.

[PreviousGenerate/review/edit/delete/export payouts](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z/billing)
[NextAdd your brand information](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/add-your-brand-information)
