# Add your brand information | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/add-your-brand-information#id-1.-add-your-brand-information)

1\. Add your brand information


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is where you can add your own branding to make your affiliate program more professional. The **logo**, **brand name**, **store domain**, and **favicon** set up here will then be displayed on your affiliate portal pages, affiliate accounts, and so on.

You must go to **Settings** \> **Branding**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fjz7EKuW8uKOc347ksVmH%252FScreenshot_57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd7e44cc-3464-444e-969c-3f18f80d1dca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c3022f73&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FxLU8oGQX5CTzVOzoRj2T%252FScreenshot_58.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddaa5e720-7b7d-41ab-8ee6-53d80d9f5241&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eda5eebe&sv=2)

You can also add your **social link**s so that affiliates reach out to you more easily!

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F8aEYrFb4SaVoLLOdUnRm%252FScreenshot_59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6dcfbea-a77e-49b5-a3fb-8dc672183383&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4fde44e3&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/add-your-brand-information#id-2.-edit-your-portal-domain)

2\. Edit your portal domain


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is where you can change your affiliate portal domain name. You'll first need to go to **Settings** > **Affiliate portal** and click this **Edit** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FHlysEoAOmZ8BpaKIiecb%252FScreenshot_60.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d4a28c3-f9f0-4fd7-85f5-82b0382c67f3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7dd007a5&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FKkafeUgm5fiH88JYTLay%252FScreenshot_61.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a044ba4-8dfc-4c5b-8da1-d60bd086321b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=368fddc7&sv=2)

Here, you can effortlessly generate, meticulously review, promptly delete, and conveniently export payouts with unparalleled efficiency.

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can go to **Payouts** > **Approved balance** to generate payouts.

# Promotional materials | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

This is where you can upload unlimited images, links, videos, and files for affiliates to use in social media promotions. Affiliates will then be able to view, copy, and download these promotional materials and distribute them to their audiences. Each file must be **under 5MB** in size.

To upload **Creatives**, you must first click the **New Creative** button and select a file type.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FmHYtAmCUQiRZkDDdTsfQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def4fb5ce-12fe-44f7-8d19-9c107597120b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a752983&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FMhVWA1cfwfIZMfPbOXpx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58f95586-2c76-48d4-86a5-b3bf9f58d650&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f34d4a4e&sv=2)

Now fill in all required information. If you want to create categories to group the materials, just type the **Category** name in.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fx3Blt0Fz3gfEJSVGzW1L%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e12e908-97e4-4b82-9a0e-445874d4e501&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fce279a2&sv=2)

The promotional materials you uploaded in **Creatives** will be displayed in the **Link & Assets** > **Media** tab on the **Affiliate Dashboard**.

[PreviousAffiliate leaderboard](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/affiliate-leaderboard)
[NextPrivacy](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/privacy)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Privacy | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

This is where you can include **Terms & Conditions** and **Privacy Policy** in your program, ensuring that affiliates can read the policies before signing up and review them anytime. Once enabled, they are automatically displayed in the footer of your **Sign-up Page** and **Affiliate Dashboard**.

To enable **Terms & Conditions** and **Privacy Policy**, you must first click this **Activate** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F1WK24nL7uiAA9XDb5Hen%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4e52807-fdc0-4be9-ac28-06b8ab4d4b1a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46e8445f&sv=2)

You can use our sample directly or add your own version! After that, click the **Save** button.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/privacy#faq)

FAQ

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/privacy#how-can-affiliates-know-about-your-policies-and-their-updates)

How can affiliates know about your policies and their updates?

First, once you activate your policies, affiliates can view them on the **sign-up page**'s sign-up form before deciding to submit their affiliate registrations.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FddmZrS58R8624fn8Thim%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c2bca2c-997b-4c59-9c56-cc96b095bdda&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13353aff&sv=2)

Once their registrations are approved, affiliates will have access to their **Affiliate Dashboard** which allows them to review the policies from time to time.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F7MIePGSPZHjfplWdS0HZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5384860-e913-4f5a-82c6-6d8343b9f0b2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=41a9582a&sv=2)

[PreviousPromotional materials](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/creatives)
[NextPrevent indexing](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/prevent-indexing)

# Languages | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

This is where you can set up the language(s) to be displayed on the **Affiliate Dashboard**, with **10 languages** available for you to choose from. English is set up as the default language and you can change that here, or add more languages in case your affiliates need more than just one default language.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Flg9KksKgia8eSguKnxsz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7d595b2-521b-4f5c-a429-d78ea11658bd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4a80eea2&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F2lPfBoRFpHvW1Co9J8vm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded625892-656b-4a4e-b6bf-4eb2bdc84a76&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a43f4204&sv=2)

You can also save affiliates some time selecting a language to be shown in their account by enabling this **Auto detect language from the browser** option. We will automatically detect a language based on the affiliate's browser.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FF70lYisVEb2Tlhwz7Z8Q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7777115-5c2c-424d-9b25-10bc35ebad9b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12a636c6&sv=2)

If the detected language isn't on our list, the default language of your affiliate portal will be displayed.

Finally, click **Save**!

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/languages#example)

Example

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FO7XZka4FCmKARgmvscX1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De474a07f-ae41-46c9-8972-1880edcf589a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4da5e4ff&sv=2)

In this example, this is how the language select menu is displayed on the Affiliate Dashboard after English was set up as the default language while Spanish and French were added as optional languages.

# Add payment methods | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

To set up payment methods for your programs, go to **Settings** \> **Payments** \> **Payment method**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FAUl8aI5hzt2RYdzM3aqY%252FScreenshot_38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62d18f8d-d6a0-4941-8095-01401aa47da7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ee6a702&sv=2)

Now it's your affiliates' turn to select which method they want to get their commissions paid with from the options available as set up above if you want them to (most recommended when you enable only multiple methods in the first place). When they log in, this notification requiring them to add payment information will show up. Affiliates must first click the **Add now** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FRSPtTosxXHO61An3efjA%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=422f6781&sv=2)

They will be redirected to this **Payment settings** tab - where they can select a payment method they prefer from the list of available methods you offer.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FZYgbrs5HQCiEdnVoU4n1%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4393a61f&sv=2)

You can also send an email reminding the affiliate to select a payment method like this:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F2Dk8qz6f1rNGQY01ufb6%252FScreenshot_39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6118f04f-42f4-427c-b3f1-cef4bd43d33d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1ad83fc4&sv=2)

You can now go to the **Payouts** tab and proceed with the commission payments!

[PreviousReports](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/reports)
[NextHow to add payment methods](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/add-payment-methods/how-to-add-payment-methods)

# Let potential affiliates find you via BixGrow Marketplace | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

By listing on our **Marketplace**, affiliates can browse for affiliate programs and join yours easily. These are information that we require to have your program listed in our **Marketplace**:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F4EDx0GJv3kWalWajZNyc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8a5b8cce-3c60-4ddb-9ff0-09ee36c7e972&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7f19ae56&sv=2)

*   Select a _program_ that you want to list
    
*   Select up to 3 _business categories_
    
*   Fill in your _brand description_
    
*   Select the _location_ where your products/services are available
    
*   List some _featured products_ (optional)
    
*   Add _search terms_ so that affiliates can find your offer easily (optional)
    

Finally, click **Save**. You'll see your program available for affiliates to browse [**here**](https://marketplace.bixgrow.com/)
. You can preview your listing and make further edits if needed!

[PreviousBuild your affiliate network with Multi-level Marketing](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing)
[NextPost-purchase Widget](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/post-purchase-widget)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Notification for you | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

1\. Contact info


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is where you can edit your **Contact Name** and **Email Address**. This contact info will be displayed on the **Affiliate Dashboard** for your affiliates to see and reach out, so it's recommended that you insert your affiliate specialist's contact here.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FNgsEaXqRldqSaHkAcFXA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e3455d8-7d57-446d-b48a-39f6ef867e15&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebd6c010&sv=2)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Ff8aatnpcRZKRJtYAA9GV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D492c6b7c-5a8b-4fb5-acc3-9657cb06421a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d20b99e1&sv=2)

Since these emails are for quick notifying purposes, they contain only basic information and can **NOT** be customized.

# Add/Approve/Deny/Import a conversion | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/add-approve-deny-a-conversion#id-1.-approve)

1\. Approve

To manually approve a commission, you must click this **Approve** button. The commission status will then become **Approved**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FreCGOEXcUci0miu2nNDq%252FScreenshot_66.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded6bc9d7-8b48-4eda-8f3e-4da63ceccd45&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0aeb07b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/add-approve-deny-a-conversion#id-2.-deny)

2\. Deny

To manually deny a commission, you must click this **Deny** button. The commission status will then become **Denied**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FTjq07EhuKPO2KuycMebe%252FScreenshot_67.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13aeaed7-e183-465e-83c7-b982bd0cc52a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cab6804f&sv=2)

After you approve or deny a commission, if you change your mind, you can always switch it to the other status by selecting the order. It's possible as long as the order's payout hasn't been made!

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FVbWgghuELcjHUEYKQQdT%252FScreenshot_68.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22ee9f0f-bcd2-410d-afb1-acc6c588f312&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28cf7817&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/add-approve-deny-a-conversion#id-3.-check-commission-details)

3\. Check commission details

Explore comprehensive commission details with just a click, empowering you to track and manage earnings with precision.

You must go to **Conversions** \> **Referral orders** and click on the order number.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FECLklktVfTuUF7VpjY8z%252FScreenshot_22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb99ea02-6ae8-43d8-90e5-6330d60f2089&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1481c408&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F5F9JCaRW29mvcz9mixFo%252FScreenshot_24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a6a2ecb-6773-4833-b441-c9df00032832&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba9ed25e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/add-approve-deny-a-conversion#id-4.-adjust-commission)

4\. Adjust commission

With this feature, you can fine-tune commission amounts of orders manually.

You must first go to **Conversions** \> **Referral orders** and click on the order number, then enter the desired adjusted amount in **Merchant adjustmen**t.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FW16qzEqPDhILi55ABlcO%252FScreenshot_25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa6b23f9-babf-4e5b-aad4-ca80cb44efe4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c093ef5c&sv=2)

Please enter a **positive value to increase** the commission and a **negative value to decrease** the commission.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/add-approve-deny-a-conversion#id-5.-auto-approve-orders)

5\. Auto-approve orders

Effortlessly manage and expedite the order approval process, ensuring smooth operations and timely commission payouts.

You must go to **Settings** \> **General**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fj8XdUNIAnylRLF9sHTet%252FScreenshot_26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59263dd1-597b-4e6c-89ae-8c5446a7a825&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a79b36c2&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/add-approve-deny-a-conversion#id-6.-export-conversions)

6\. Export conversions

Seamlessly export conversion data to analyze, optimize, and strategize effectively, empowering you to make data-driven decisions for your affiliate program's success.

You must go to **Conversions** \> **Referral orders** \> **Export**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F9wdMwV3KM7IjiiJ1tOUE%252FScreenshot_27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dffd2996d-3ad3-4820-bb5c-a84e213beae0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12586f97&sv=2)

You can choose to export either **All conversions** or just **Filtered conversions**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fqszj8aFsNohynDNjNbd0%252FScreenshot_28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1729ad71-4fe5-4dcb-9a50-2dfbb16e4575&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=52621848&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/add-approve-deny-a-conversion#id-7.-import-conversions)

7\. Import conversions

You can bulk import up to 250 orders per file into your programs. This is extremely useful when you migrate from another app.

This feature is **enabled upon request for eligible users only**. We require a legit order list and a subscription to a paid plan.

To do so, you must first contact us to enable the **Import** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FIBtYP1pnf2NZHCUdL74g%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D496ac7a9-d2cf-428b-964b-54a292159a8f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d8b1495&sv=2)

1.  Upload your CSV file (_Order Number_, _Affiliate Email_, _Order Total_, _Affiliate Commission_, and _Order Status_ columns are required)
    
2.  Click **Import orders**
    

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FNHbNe5n0cIA6nsWmJ37l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77d627c6-676f-4c27-9f88-974afa4c971a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7eee6e86&sv=2)

**Download our sample CSV file** to set up your data field columns correctly!

You can also **import customers** the same way - doesn't require a feature request.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fc9SFUiNm8eNfwdLHi8Rk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1a94d50-094d-42bc-9913-b9d3f406ace5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b5c022d&sv=2)

[NextHow conversions are tracked](https://docs.bixgrow.com/conversions/how-conversions-are-tracked)

# Gifts | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Gifts are free products or discounts that you can send to affiliates as a welcome gesture when they join the affiliate program or as a performance bonus that doesn't require a trigger condition.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/gifts#id-1.-set-up-and-send-gifts-automatically)

1\. Set up and send gifts automatically

To set up a Gift, you must first go to **Extra functions** > **Gifts** \> **Create gift**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fy7szt52ghzVvdFCF4E8U%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84234f91-8819-4293-8f9c-16819f69b140&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bbf0ebe7&sv=2)

Next, to label this gift, please input the **Gift name**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FzrbgzTILC6MMM1pv3a0e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56c4f797-2e17-4f24-bc73-c0602211f3c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81a70645&sv=2)

If you'd like to automatically send gifts to affiliates when they join your program(s), check the box and select the program(s) for which you want to deliver gifts to newly registered affiliates.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FaoSQf7LV9mFPrFPZj9VE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4376a61-2e0b-4504-a168-ba83fa9fc387&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f83e834a&sv=2)

You can choose either a free _Product_ or a _Discount code_ as the **Gift type**. The free _Product_ option allows affiliates to receive product(s) at no cost, while the _Discount code_ option provides them with a discount on selected products, with the discount amount set by you.

Here, you browse for product(s) that the gift should apply to.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fnh5om6cY8wG9IeR4ZWOe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3bbd0dd6-b210-48fa-a2a3-1c90b4e51fe5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c09ab36&sv=2)

Then please click **Add**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FRNlpamirHHmYDuJsg1bH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e1cf6a4-60f4-4cae-9566-718515318269&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6c5072af&sv=2)

You must also input the maximum quantity of each product and the number of products each affiliate can claim per order.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FNIacEg7oZmUaEAAQgXCY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d323043-c9b6-4286-9bca-b5136426bc83&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=235e8bad&sv=2)

In this example, each affiliate can claim two products per gift/order, with a maximum of 1 Sponge Cupke, 2 Sponge Cloudee, and 1 Sponge Choco.

Finally, click **Save**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F8gehmvmmt15vFI1NTbAc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56b6b7e4-cb81-4158-ab8d-7949fb0dbe7a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1fc2f800&sv=2)

If you select the **Gift type** as _Discount code_, the gifts will equal **Personal coupons**. By checking the _Automatically send this gift_ box, you can have personal coupons auto-generated for newly registered affiliates.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FoCwo1IWZgyKRZ19rsh4B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c4fa695-ecf7-4cf3-bb1d-528db300afcf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=562720c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/gifts#id-2.-send-gifts-manually)

2\. Send gifts manually

Besides auto-generating gifts for newly registered affiliates, you can also send gifts manually to selected affiliate(s) at the same time.

Here, please click on **Send gift**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F5KlICXd7sC1f93ilyGA9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D51f8677d-e622-4f09-a0aa-091e6b9ccb19&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e3e8d84f&sv=2)

And select affiliates that should receive these gifts manually. Finally, click **Send gifts**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FhSjDD90FI38LhsRBcfpu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28c4aca8-3299-4615-a2ca-a26fc88298bb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14c8ec61&sv=2)

This is a sample result

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FYhLsf1XqbRWABcTOdEVS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6f21306-b469-4d73-81aa-7376d1a60720&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64b0df52&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/gifts#id-3.-claim-gifts)

3\. Claim gifts

As an affiliate, I can claim my gift in the affiliate admin section.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FpFOPA1y692AajClxVaRw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4e265d7-843f-4822-a952-fa7a1aa6e48f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd4b6da1&sv=2)

Please click **Redeem**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FFK7VsiSQzOfT1jBgqXOp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2812e51-464a-4951-b51b-294687c2f1c0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea6e8d18&sv=2)

As I'm allowed to claim one product from the available gifts, I'll proceed with selecting a product I want and fill in my shipping information. Finally, I click on the **Redeem** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FHcqxfPM9nbBtrY2xdl88%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D613651e0-c6e4-4e77-85d9-8e34f0063c8a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d8fef65&sv=2)

This is a sample result

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FJCcHXCTCog1ZPgZXWuns%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e702802-ab4d-4a9e-b2a9-cf7aa2aa516c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f4ec0295&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FOMy4WnsD3T6gBOMfc8Bs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43b2c31b-8fcf-47ef-b0f2-2e42b38cbec4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5b72c68a&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/gifts#id-4.-check-gifts-redeem-status)

4\. Check gifts' redeem status

Here in **Gifts history**, you can see whether a gift has been **Sent** (not yet redeemed), **Canceled** (before redeeming), or **Redeemed**. If successfully redeemed, there will also be information regarding the gift's actual value in use and its order number.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FKs9AI6Mzgu3C9kNsEx6G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dae6fd9ac-0f04-47f4-80fa-0719c771bca8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e9139cac&sv=2)

# Staff accounts | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Creating staff accounts allows your staff to be granted customized access to **BixGrow** and helps you with affiliate marketing management. They will log in via a staff-only portal, which means you won't have to grant your staff Shopify store access for them to log in to **BixGrow** and they'll have no control over your store except for the granted app permissions.

You will first need to click this **Add staff** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FS9jiIOEF0NrsUkGjMMbm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ce1748b-3603-40b8-8f26-2a0f52b4fd3b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=266eb372&sv=2)

There, you fill in the staff account's information and grant all or limited permissions to your preference.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FsKjwoatH1uwebKMpNtq9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ee6ffc6-b173-45b6-97ce-baf0d3fa1022&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6cbdb262&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/staff-accounts#example)

Example

This is the result you have after clicking the **Create** button:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FSCnuNhcCtVd4KsAOaJzb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D924ec8ee-cba7-4a08-bc4b-bce48bd6414e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=68f13845&sv=2)

This is how a staff-only portal will look like:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fj4GfrFNPn3ZzhDO1u2Zu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db129e7c6-5e8c-4192-8c43-1f855a195b9a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=127dda60&sv=2)

You can leave the **Store's Shopify URL** field blank if you don't have multiple stores. In case you have multiple stores and your staff has access to more than one of them, the field will be **required**.

[PreviousPayPal](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/paypal)
[NextAdvanced](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/advanced)

Last updated 1 year ago

# FAQ | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/faq#why-do-i-no-longer-see-the-referral-displays-i-set-up-in-my-store-im-sure-theyre-still-turned-on)

Why do I no longer see the referral displays I set up in my store? I'm sure they're still turned on.

In the **Starter** (free) plan, we offer _up to 30 advocate accounts_ for the referral program. If your number of advocate signups exceeds this quota, all your referral displays will be temporarily disabled until you upgrade to a paid plan and release the limit.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FAWGN5F5KsReKB5KpX5Yb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4e1f2e9-1fa2-4028-bba3-b0980005d077&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61ebdb1&sv=2)

[PreviousFriend Reward Pop-up](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/friend-reward-pop-up)
[NextManage advocate accounts](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/manage-advocate-accounts)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Display your affiliate portal on the storefront | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/display-on-the-storefront#display-your-page-on-the-storefront)

Display your page on the storefront

To add a portal page to your store's menu, you must first go to your Shopify account > **Content** > **Menus**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FsS0Xhx8LlnDKUaEJFhJd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ba0faaf-6772-4be0-9df3-b186faea1eee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bd5affe2&sv=2)

Select a **menu** in which you want to put the page.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FRTYaKmnTGa2L8qDA9uGp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D160c79f6-6775-4c85-9462-0519a606fcda&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b25b984&sv=2)

Now click **Add menu item**. Then, enter a **Label** for it and paste the portal page's link that you've just **copied in BixGrow**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FJq3bwLaFGPzu6a8AdtEk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56f0a936-dabd-4bfd-ba01-fb9298d8433d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ecfbf606&sv=2)

Finally, click **Save** to update your changes.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FrTbcCo7nqd6WwSxrAqpi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd230730d-d5fd-4998-8b43-41cfdcf15c5d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7a47656&sv=2)

This is a sample result:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FpVu26ouqmuibq2aufLkZ%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96b09119&sv=2)

Please keep in mind that while the **Landing page** and **Log-in page** are the same for all programs, the **Sign-up pages** are different for each program. Therefore, the Sign-up page's link you copy in the app belongs only to your **default program**.

[PreviousCustomize your affiliate portal](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/customize)
[NextEmbed your affiliate portal into the store](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/embed-on-the-storefront)

# In-app Payment | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

You can **pay affiliates directly within BixGrow** using **PayPal** (integration required) or **Store Credit**.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z/in-app-payment#a.-paypal-payment-process)

A. PayPal payment process


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**1.** The **merchant** selects **PayPal** [**here**](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/add-payment-methods)
 then goes to **Settings** > **Integration** and sets up **PayPal integration** (a step-by-step guide on how to integrate your PayPal account [**here**](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/paypal)
).

**2.** **BixGrow** provides a **PayPal** information form for your **affiliates** to fill in their **PayPal** emails.

**3.** The **merchant** generates a payout and pays the corresponding commission in-app with **PayPal**.

**4.** **BixGrow** sends the affiliate an email notification of the **PayPal** payout including payment details.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z/in-app-payment#b.-make-paypal-payments)

B. Make PayPal payments


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you have successfully integrated your **PayPal** account with **BixGrow** in **step 1**, this is **step 3** where you can make in-app payments. You can pay one or all affiliates (that selected PayPal) at a time using **Bulk mode**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FsCTVpQEaTelYsG071Mw2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddeffc4ae-4ba4-44a1-8de0-13a3f2b25b0c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36628006&sv=2)

You must first fill in the email subject (for the payout notification email) and click the **Pay with PayPal** button.

Now enter the Payment Password you set up while integrating and click this **Pay now** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FLdPSlW0rNlQEraFj25dH%252FScreenshot_87.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7bc81a4-0edd-4389-9b2b-94d71a689060&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3211d100&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z/in-app-payment#store-credit)

STORE CREDIT


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z/in-app-payment#a.-store-credit-payment-process)

A. Store Credit payment process


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**1.** The **merchant** selects **Store Credit** and set up how affiliates can generate coupons using the **Store Credit** balance they have [**here**](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/add-payment-methods)
.

**2.** The **merchant** generates a payout and adds credits to affiliates' balance in-app.

**3.** **BixGrow** sends the affiliate an email notification of the Store Credit payout including payment details.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z/in-app-payment#b.-make-store-credit-payments)

B. Make Store Credit payments


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**By default, you** allow affiliates to generate coupons using the store credits they have. Click this **Pay with Store Credit** button to add the credit to the affiliate's Store Credit balance.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F2aPPF7t0qyh2mZOof1Lc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D846912d3-d9ca-48c2-9257-0b762b5d3e36&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d99d2915&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FPvk6q5rqJkAHA40T4SKH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62a131d4-dac2-439b-b4e8-5cfa679e195f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b6387d4&sv=2)

The Store Credit balance will appear in the **Affiliate dashboard** as follows:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FpN3kn0x69BhN8h0IiscH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D88fd6c46-4513-4c30-864e-ed582d264eff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b63c008&sv=2)

To redeem coupons with the Store Credit balance, affiliates must first click on **Redeem coupon**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fghb6rlYgQ69gz20fQ3Bm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5e6e16f-3f04-434f-8ff3-b88dd92627e2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a3de082e&sv=2)

There, affiliates can enter the Store Credit amount that they want to redeem, and click this **Get coupon** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F9H5F6WliCp17sSz6lDrR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5c689d52-7bc6-4ed0-9751-fdf737bae40c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12fbc78f&sv=2)

The coupon redeemed with Store Credit will look like this:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F8Y1OmczQ7xYIqKwdcjrN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e1c17e0-2f47-4692-9e93-37ed779f0971&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89b098bf&sv=2)

# Affiliate portal tracking | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

If you're looking to track affiliate signups, logins, and page visits, you can integrate either **Google Tag Manager (GTM)** or **Facebook Pixel** into your affiliate portal.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fl6MPmEsT6QMC2hcSgrAV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da9c12c7c-0ca5-4a8a-89ec-2631c61a7cc2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd15a999&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/affiliate-portal-tracking#id-1.-google-tag-manager)

1\. Google Tag Manager

**a. Get your Container ID** If you don’t already have a GTM account:

*   Go to https://tagmanager.google.com
    
*   Click **Create Account**
    
*   Set up a container for your Shopify store
    
*   Choose **Web** as the target platform
    
*   After setup, you will receive a GTM ID like `GTM-XXXXXXX`
    

**b. Enter your GTM ID**

*   In Shopify admin, go to **Affiliate Portal Tracking**
    
*   Click on **Google Tag Manager**
    
*   Enter your **GTM Container ID**
    
*   _(Optional)_ Enter a **Signup Conversion Event** name (e.g., `affiliate_signup`)
    
*   Click **Save**
    

**c. Create a Custom event trigger**

*   In GTM, go to **Triggers** → **New**
    
*   Choose trigger type: **Custom Event**
    
*   Event name: match the one you entered above (e.g., `affiliate_signup`)
    
*   Save the trigger
    

**d. Create a Tag to fire on signup**

*   Go to **Tags** → **New**
    
*   Choose a tag type (e.g., Google Ads Conversion Tracking, GA4 Event, etc.)
    
*   Link the trigger from step 3
    
*   Save and publish your container
    

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/affiliate-portal-tracking#id-2.-facebook-pixel)

2\. Facebook Pixel

**a. Create your Facebook Pixel ID**

*   Go to Facebook Events Manager
    
*   Click **Connect Data Sources** → Choose **Web**
    
*   Select **Facebook Pixel** and click **Connect**
    
*   Follow the steps and you will get a **Pixel ID** (a long numeric string)
    

**b. Enter your Pixel ID**

*   In Shopify admin, go to **Affiliate Portal Tracking**
    
*   Click on **Facebook Pixel**
    
*   Enter your **Pixel ID**
    
*   _(Optional)_ Enter a **Signup Conversion Event** (e.g., `AffiliateSignup`)
    
*   Click **Save**
    

**c. Set up a Custom Event**

*   After a signup, the app will send a `fbq('trackCustom', 'AffiliateSignup')` event (or your chosen event name)
    
*   In **Events Manager**, go to **Custom Conversions**
    
*   Click **Create Custom Conversion**
    
    *   Select your Pixel
        
    *   Set **Event Name** = your custom event (e.g., `AffiliateSignup`)
        
    *   Add rules if needed (e.g., URL contains `/signup-success`)
        
    *   Click **Create**
        
    

*   You can use GTM to manage both Google Ads and Facebook Pixel centrally.
    
*   Use the signup event to create retargeting audiences, optimize conversions, or measure ad performance.
    
*   GTM and Facebook Pixel both support debugging tools like **Tag Assistant** and **Pixel Helper** for troubleshooting.
    

[PreviousPrevent indexing](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/prevent-indexing)
[NextNotification for you](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/notification-for-you)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Customize your affiliate portal | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

To customize your affiliate portal, you must first go to **Settings** \> **Affiliate portal** > **Portal pages** > **Customize**. You can always see the preview right below whenever you make changes.

# Toolbars | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

With **Toolbars** that display affiliates' basic information, customers will be able to know exactly which affiliate they're shopping with and crediting their purchases to.

To display **Toolbars** in your store, you must first allow BixGrow to embed in your theme by clicking this **Enable now** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FExSwwEH7I1qSToSEZtC4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46bea765-96ad-438d-93ff-1d5039637518&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8dac01be&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/toolbars#id-1.-announcement-bar)

1\. Announcement Bar

This display shows up as a text bar in the header of your storefront. You can edit its content freely using the provided tags, e.g. "You are shopping with {first\_name} - @{instagram} on Instagram".

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FD9yOu17XVcMovXpQZm1g%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db60b2a5e-f4ab-40c3-ab1d-d2629c904c06&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71bcec24&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/toolbars#example)

Example

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FggiX8W7CPGIw5mU16Mbg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c68e45e-1cd8-4301-b62d-65672dc72834&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a0042f4e&sv=2)

This is how the **Announcement Bar** is displayed once enabled with the "You are shopping with {full\_name}" content.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/toolbars#id-2.-floating-widget)

**2\. Floating Widget**

This display shows up as a text + avatar widget in the footer of your storefront. You can edit its content freely using the provided tags, e.g. "{first\_name} - @{tiktok} on TikTok".

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FLogQ3b6y9UlH48NVnvF1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D716f3527-fcd0-4dcf-848b-50686ee866c1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1eaf1c95&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/toolbars#example-1)

# What is a Referral Program? | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

A Referral Program - compared to an Affiliate Program - is a simpler way for happy customers to share your products with their friends and family. The structure is quick to set up, and no marketing experience or payment methods are required.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FSCSk8baxlyv5rxEFr0ky%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf30bc50-3bb7-4ff1-bcc0-b9767e0f38a1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=597f4e02&sv=2)

One can be found in **Extra functions** \> **Others**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FmJD9GTMfq1ZzlTbLtdfF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07a846c8-4139-4d0f-bbaa-4d074d61254b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6df6ad9a&sv=2)

# Review referrals | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

An **advocate reward** is given when an order is recorded to be placed via a **friend discount**, which was generated by the **advocate link**. The order also had to be **paid** or **marked as paid** on Shopify. When these conditions are met, the order is considered a **referral** and is tracked in this table. There are the order's date, order number, the advocate who brought the order, the friend who placed the order, the order's total sale, the reward status, and the friend discount code that was used.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fq2sparNs84RTjCCmjMT6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6d5441d-de2d-47d1-9891-4429b9408e92&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a36039b5&sv=2)

The reward status will change from **Approved** to **Suspended** automatically if a return/refund for the order on Shopify is detected and no **advocate reward** will be given.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FSa2SMrFfvHuunHv3dt6F%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd12979b0-ab2f-410c-ab51-c753eaed63a1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b4c6ca6&sv=2)

[PreviousManage advocate accounts](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/manage-advocate-accounts)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Settings | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/set-up-your-program/settings#id-2.-referral-landing-page)

**1\.** Referral landing page


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A **landing page** is a URL that you want advocates to share and promote your products or services. All default advocate links in the program will be generated following this format.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Ffiles.gitbook.com%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Mcrh8g2NluDX_batYq7%252Fuploads%252FnElmGxYgSyUvZJTxfbbs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e9c0138-712b-4597-a5f5-5b116fcd4c27&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6c436b5b&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/set-up-your-program/settings#id-3.-fraud-protection)

**2\. Fraud protection**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Fraud Protection** prevents your advocates from misusing your programs by referring themselves and earning rewards. This feature can help you avoid fraud by blocking commission if a suspicious referral is detected. We provide three types of **Fraud Protection**:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FACxmOdYPiZ0ifDFjKjkV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D51feab91-89e6-45b5-800b-90e3d8171619&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d9567ec6&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/set-up-your-program/settings#a.-same-email-address)

**a. Same email address**

Your advocates' rewards will be prevented if both their and their friends’ email addresses are the same.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/set-up-your-program/settings#b.-same-ip)

b**. Same IP**

Your advocates’ rewards will be prevented if their and their friends’ IP addresses are the same (for IP address is a unique number assigned to a device, having the same IP address most probably means using the same device).

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/set-up-your-program/settings#c.-same-first-name-and-last-name)

**c. Same first name and last name**

Your advocates’ rewards will be prevented if their and their friends’ first and last names are the same.

Please keep in mind that there still is a possibility of two different people sharing the same first and last name.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/set-up-your-program/settings#id-3.-assign-tags-to-orders-customers-on-shopify)

**3\.** Assign tags to orders/customers on Shopify


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This feature can help you tell referral orders from normal orders on Shopify by adding specific referral tags to them.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F7pAma8orfIyWQ5LgFFBe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dae9ba3ba-23a0-4e45-9227-d4e435fff24e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a12560f&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/set-up-your-program/settings#id-5.-language)

**5\. Language**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is where you can set up multiple languages of the Referral **Displays** for advocates and their friends/customers to see (**Widget**, **Custom Page**, **Post-purchase Pop-up**, and **Email**). There are **10 languages** available for you to choose from and will only work if your store supports multi-language.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fsx0Ts9XEWW7udp5cCUyo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22050472-e470-4406-a632-31854d5a2412&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d26beb87&sv=2)

[PreviousRewards](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/set-up-your-program/rewards)
[NextAttract advocates to sign up for your program](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program)

# Build your affiliate network with Multi-level Marketing | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing#id-1.-what-is-mlm)

1\. What is MLM?

**MLM**, also known as **network marketing** or **referral marketing**, is a promising strategy to sell products and services by encouraging existing employees or affiliates to recruit new affiliates. As a result, your business could reach out to more potential clients via a variety of channels and advertising campaigns.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FxHBJa78s8LqCyzmA2Buc%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85d5430a&sv=2)

MLM Model

The fundamental of **MLM** is represented by a pyramid, in which each affiliate asks another affiliate to join his or her affiliate network system at a downline level. The more people who are invited, the more products or services will be able to reach out to their target market.

Having MLM set up in your affiliate program means each affiliate in the pyramid network is not only paid for the sales he/she generates but also for a share of the sales made by their downline affiliates - which is called **network commission**. Therefore, people in the network would be incentivized to recruit more affiliates under them instead of just directly selling products to customers.

The network commission that upline affiliates receive will be provided **separately**, **not deducted** from the commission of the downline affiliate.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing#id-2.-how-to-set-up)

2\. How to set up

To set up **MLM**, you must first go to **Extra functions** > **Multi-level Marketing (MLM)** and click the **Activate MLM** checkbox.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FHIRNbqA170GeO417DA9B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5078a26f-b110-4767-aeb0-79ffb1232ae8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=348de878&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FwjrV5QSB6pyf4MKSsiDe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da9339d8e-2b10-455e-abe1-205e308c02d7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0c361d0&sv=2)

The maximum of MLM levels is **20**. It's recommended that there are fewer than 5 levels as it will be easier for you to manage the network connections and calculate how much total commission you're willing to pay on an order.

**Network commission** can be based on total sale or program commission, and set at a percentage or flat rate. The commission value should be set in descending order to make sure that the affiliate who directly brought the order will receive the most commission amount. You can take a look at the **Live example** to check if you set up everything correctly!

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing#example)

Example

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FL78pSi1VjuGytLr18h9d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f5ef077-4560-41a9-879d-ebee74c949dc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7f35d9c2&sv=2)

In this example, William invited Quinn and Quinn invited James, which makes William and Quinn both James' parent affiliates. The **MLM** structure is applied to all affiliates in the "Gold" program and there are two network commission levels. There is a 10% default commission for James - the downline affiliate who brought the order and two network commissions for Quinn and William based on their levels - 5% (Quinn: level 1) and 3% (William: level 2). The total amount of commission that needs to be paid for this $100 order is $18.

You can also configure advanced settings like a **recruitment bonus** to your affiliates when they successfully recruit other affiliates or the **minimum total revenue** an affiliate must reach to be able to receive network commission. Or **select a program for the invited affiliates** to join if you don't want them to start at the same level as the upline affiliate.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FYlO4VDfQ2qV6DHwmUZVT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f2ce036-c888-48c2-a84c-d4ad87739207&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=934a8cfa&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing#example-1)

Example

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FnO5WJiyBZBDTpAwmT54x%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b1d779f-c92d-41b3-aad1-dd2e3d56ae27&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca5f2f4d&sv=2)

In this example, the **MLM** **recruitment bonus** is $5 and the **minimum total revenue** is $50. Quinn ("Affiliate" program) recruited James and received a $5 bonus. James is automatically placed in the "TEST" program. When James brings back an order, Quinn has only generated $40 of personal sales and is not eligible to receive a 5% **network commission** for that order although being James' parent affiliate.

Once you are done with the settings, remember to click **Save**!

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing#id-3.-how-affiliates-recruit-others)

3\. How affiliates recruit others

After MLM is **activated**, each **Affiliate Dashboard** will have a **network link**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FVJNdX69L1v7mImCMtB6Q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db8c9bf67-4c5d-4cd2-b7c7-0dcd47b46d56&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=706ad568&sv=2)

Affiliates will share their dedicated **network links** to recruit others to join your program. When they click a **network link** and sign up as new affiliates, they will be considered as **downline affiliates** of a lower level than the link owner. Plus, downline affiliates' performances can be viewed in both the merchant's and the upline affiliates' dashboards.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing#faq)

FAQ

**Q**: **Is a network link different from an affiliate link?**

A: Yes, it is. Here are their differences:

Network link

Affiliate link

**Format**

Typically _yourdomain.bixgrow.com/register?parent=..._

Typically _yourdomain?bg\_ref=..._ (default) or _yourdomain/affiliate\_name_ (shortened)

**What affiliates use it for**

Inviting more affiliates to join the **MLM** network. Invited affiliates will automatically become their downlines, allowing them to earn networks commissions on the downlines' sales.

Driving customers and sales to your store. **Referral orders** made directly using affiliate links allow them to earn commissions.

**Where to find**

**Affiliate admin** \> **Network** \> **Network link**

**Affilate profile** or **Affiliate admin** > **Affiliate link**

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing#id-4.-set-a-parent-for-an-existing-affiliate)

4\. Set a parent for an existing affiliate

If you want to set upline affiliates for an existing affiliate, go to **Affiliates** \> click the affiliate's name > **Network** \> **Set Parent**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FyoDgSK6x4V6WzQlUTiKi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2521cdb-2696-4f69-a08d-76c935556411&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5870e822&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fnmw2nE2Fy5zePhuDeN46%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43117f87-c9c3-4e72-aed7-eb6672264a58&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9771c455&sv=2)

Here, you can fill in the parent affiliate's name or email to search. When you finish, click **Save.**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FKwVxmcK9h1P4qErMXYPy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5347068a-cda6-4263-b3fc-d49eb07899fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=25275308&sv=2)

There can only be **one** direct upline affiliate for each affiliate.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing#id-5.-how-an-mlm-commission-is-displayed)

5\. How an MLM commission is displayed

If an order is brought by an affiliate in the MLM network, the order commission for the downline as well as the network commission for the upline will be shown in **Conversions**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F3BKlvo1MWf6sV6R2NOXg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0413f81f-caad-48d8-a126-0a30b034852f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dad219c6&sv=2)

Affiliates can also keep track of their network commissions also in the **Network** tab.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing#faq-1)

FAQ

**Q**: **Can I assign an affiliate to a fixed MLM level? For example, I set up A as everyone's level 1 parent affiliate?**

A: No, that is not possible. MLM levels are **NOT** fixed.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/promote-your-program/multi-level-marketing#example-2)

Example

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FaOehdtjr2F8rAsZdhjF9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc913e3d-3f5e-4393-8543-71f82d3ac26a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cb9874fb&sv=2)

Here, James is the direct affiliate who makes the sale (earns 10%), while Quinn is his level 1 parent affiliate (earns 5%), and William is his level 2 (earns 3%).

If Quinn makes a sale, she is the direct affiliate (earns 10%), while William is her level 1 parent affiliate (earns 3%), and there's no level 2 as the levels stop there.

**Conclusion**: Affiliates are at a different MLM level for each order, depending on their relationship with the affiliate who makes the sale (direct/parent/child), and the number of levels away from their parent/child affiliate. An affiliate can be the direct seller on an order, an MLM level 1 affiliate on another, and level 2 on another one at the same time.

# Advanced | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/advanced#id-1.-w-9-form)

1\. W-9 Form

This feature allows you to easily collect your U.S. affiliates' **W-9 forms** for tax filing purposes. Affiliates will get to confirm if they're U.S. residents first to determine if they must fill in this form.

You will first need to enable it by clicking this button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FUEFOH1HOjfqfbozBfxny%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd99e4418-fb5b-4ee0-8e24-6c58d5cd4c4c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2249f337&sv=2)

You can also select which email address will you receive the signed forms by clicking **Configure**.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/advanced#example)

Example

This is how a **W-9 form** is collected from an affiliate.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FxufoMdazaWSx9zf0I2Zj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f6e3569-e51e-4024-857e-79b633b2892d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aafe8ac5&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FoWjPtdCbGq3YXU7Q8kIh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb5e4e92-8eae-4d78-96d5-b2aa9582dc51&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b37b068&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/advanced#id-2.-multi-sign-up-pages)

2\. Multi sign-up pages

This is what allows you to have different sign-up pages for different affiliate programs at the same time! After enabling this feature, each program will show up with a different link in the **Programs** tab. Also, it unhides the option to select a different program for invited affiliates to join **MLM**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FOtFZoHFeoVDh6DHeALgk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd50955f5-3e44-4b3e-80aa-07584b9f18d1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a1c15bd3&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/advanced#id-3.-track-pending-referral-orders)

**3\. Track Pending Referral Orders**

This is where you can choose to **Record Pending Orders** as successful referrals even though they weren't paid for or marked as paid on Shopify.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FK2ZmesnnzRmV6q02R3gA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b48f544-5bd3-46de-b1d4-657b4332faf0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d81e866b&sv=2)

If this isn't enabled, we'll keep tracking only **Paid** orders by default.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/advanced#id-4.-report-data-optional-but-important)

4\. Report data (optional but important)

This is where you can choose which sale data should be used and displayed to your affiliates regarding commission calculation - your **Total Sales on Shopify** or **Commissionable Sales in BixGrow**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F1cKW5jgt0F20Jbe2igxo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5fcac4b3-388d-4dc2-9348-84f100cf9d31&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cc0caa1b&sv=2)

The Commissionable Sales value is usually less than of Shopify's Total Sales since it's often set up as Total Sales minus the fees.

# Manage advocate accounts | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

This is where you can manage and track your advocates' performances.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FoYIgINmIrsO4wa6wELUY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d3479fc-6169-494d-a466-c67b9132075b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a6c2afe2&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FLvc9PYbJGJhHfnAAJ7iK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dead80b3a-5536-4c12-a5e8-cf57b458130e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5486b455&sv=2)

# Friend Reward Pop-up | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

You can customize the **Pop-up** that's displayed to the friends/customers who clicked on advocate links.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FLPvXyik97nE2uQUMxc4K%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddc69d2fd-5e6e-4a91-8a7c-a4eac578856e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e3de64aa&sv=2)

This is a sample **Friend Reward Pop-up:**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FobpZEp4S5uCQeqV3dtcI%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=837a90e2&sv=2)

# Rewards | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

Usually, rewards in referral programs can be for **both advocates and friends**. With advocates, it's to motivate them to share your products with family, friends, and colleagues... Meanwhile, rewards can encourage customers so they are more likely to purchase. These two-sided rewards are recommended because it's a win-win for both advocates and friends.

This is where you can set up rewards for advocates and their friends to boost referral orders.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FryWQSa6RUTQHsIv8HjFz%252FScreenshot_106.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4ab217a-88f8-40d8-b048-f1be99955cf4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=25cf65d8&sv=2)

Coupons will be generated automatically when friends click referral links and they will have the format as you set up.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fwl4W6qwDEihImCMsWYt1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0336cb91-8ef3-4661-8793-43492dbbe028&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5f89e6d3&sv=2)

For **Rewards**, you can choose between **Percentage**, **Fixed amount**, or **Free shipping**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FOUBlCmGi5WDWzGBYKQil%252FScreenshot_105.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c4adef9-bd49-4d6a-be33-e822417612a4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=afd5f2d9&sv=2)

For example, if you set the discount value to 20%, your advocates will receive 20% discount codes each time they bring back orders.

You can also have a **minimum purchase amount** for eligible rewards, or select which **products** should be referred. An **expiration** time for the discounts can also be enabled, and if not, advocates and their friends can use these discounts whenever they want as the discounts never expire.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FOjxp8cBGOYr7cfzljAMi%252FScreenshot_104.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8aa254a4-6393-43d0-be60-4df826ef26cc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9288011c&sv=2)

You can now toggle the discounts' applicable **combinations** (with other discounts) and **purchase type** (of the order) as well.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FOBwVdmgZFZGsl1teCH8Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54d21cc3-0ca9-49e3-bb85-b6f0911b4714&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=209b4b9f&sv=2)

Please note that the **Purchase type** selection menu is **ONLY** available when you have active subscription products in your store.

The **reward send delay** helps you decide when the reward should be sent after a referral is recorded. It's recommended to match the time limit of your return policy to make sure you don't reward canceled orders. During this period, it's possible that you deny suspicious/fraudulent orders manually.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FHEKD1AzaODD1V5ZnsiZQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94c5c841-0b17-4d07-87f3-63e88294e40b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe943d56&sv=2)

[PreviousSet up your program](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/set-up-your-program)
[NextSettings](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/set-up-your-program/settings)

Last updated 1 year ago
