# Mailchimp | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

**Mailchimp** is a marketing automation software for e-commerce. You'll be able to fully automate your marketing campaigns and boost them with the support of your affiliates after the integration procedure is complete.

In order to integrate, you must first get the **Klaviyo API key** of your **Mailchimp** account.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/mailchimp#id-1.-sign-up-or-log-in-to-your-mailchimp-account)

1\. Sign up or log in to [your Mailchimp account](https://login.mailchimp.com/)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/mailchimp#id-2.-create-your-contact-list)

2\. Create your contact list

All affiliates will be added to your contact list after you create one, allowing you to manage campaigns for your team.

In case you don't have a contact list, you can add contacts by clicking **Add Your Contacts**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FCCVhcWanf1BALG2MNK3y%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8fd2a89c&sv=2)

Now go to **Audience** \> **Audience dashboard** > **Manage Audience** > **View audiences.**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F7q7MBkjcBxKzkolpyGr2%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=423ab077&sv=2)

Next, click **Create Audience**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fhqc79BDop3FhzWUqmzC8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f2ee44bf&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/mailchimp#id-3.-get-the-mailchimp-api-key-and-integrate)

3\. Get the MailChimp API key and integrate

Navigate your account setting:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FwxEgEGLr2edn2XlyVHD2%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9f8d2a39&sv=2)

Visit **Extras** tab > **API keys**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FU0RgxZs6hFIarJh0dQUM%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86831cfa&sv=2)

In the **APIs** section, click **Create a Key**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F8Uyv6lwbTcrbRp2ehb0D%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28fdbd6d&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FN1OlGrnBvNd2PtCWDN4e%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d10961bc&sv=2)

Go back to **BixGrow** > **Settings** \> **Integration** \> **Mailchimp** and click **Connect**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FlNkthzTchN50X3rBBfFs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf06a115-bb4a-443c-bbb0-25eaaca3ab60&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b819852&sv=2)

Paste the API key in and click **Next**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fq8EYLINI6Pmyedh8CCwg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D467c5550-669b-460b-a1dc-38bcd269b635&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b651974d&sv=2)

You will then be required to choose a list to sync the affiliate contacts. Once you've finished, click **Save & Sync**:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FI7c1f1BSx5ddJt0jzeax%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99c7c0b9-2791-4be0-9869-7365b051d8f3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c2d3a64c&sv=2)

[PreviousKlaviyo](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/klaviyo)
[NextPayPal](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/paypal)

# PayPal | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

**PayPal** allows you to pay your affiliates in a few seconds. Before we begin, please remember that a **PayPal Business Account** is required for integration, and this integration **does not offer automatic payouts**. [**Learn more**](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/payouts/#enable-payouts)
 about **PayPal Payouts**.

**All steps are compulsory** and none should be skipped. A tutorial video can be found here.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/paypal#step-1-log-in-to-your-paypal-account)

Step 1: Log in to [your PayPal account](https://www.paypal.com/)



--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Log in using your **PayPal** account's email address and password.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fzsbc0M0MjK6tNpD2TFEQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd692622-b174-4e3d-ac56-e2545e63b484&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b92df9a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FGZ1LTuAhjqxIWk5K2432%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debc6c5a2-d94a-447e-ab5a-7bcb3c6e66b5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0303d26&sv=2)

Here, click on **Developer** to access your **PayPal Developer Dashboard**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FUdAb7JXyFzhlbVnPWmKr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D237da28d-b432-466a-8be4-9937717af2fb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0d879ac&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F1toEyFpdgrWyNhIqH2Yt%252FScreenshot_9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6545708a-2635-43e7-9d8d-b05659c452c5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef8c47d5&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/paypal#step-2-enable-paypal-payouts)

Step 2: Enable PayPal Payouts


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Visit **My Account**, scroll down, and click **Enable** in the **Live** column.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FAL1v7FvASIO39avCSkbX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e770397&sv=2)

To get this certified, you need to contact **PayPal** (it can take from hours to days).

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Ftm7TSNXUf6gpas2NI6FT%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec845bce&sv=2)

You'll be redirected to the [**PayPal Customer Service team**](https://www.paypal.com/us/smarthelp/contact-us)
. On the **Contact** page, scroll down and click on **Call us** or **Message Center** > **New Message**, then initiate a chat with their team so they can assist you further.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FjBn25syIbtXVcZWGAvpG%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48747109&sv=2)![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FzgoVxzyAz7NH9nwHmLNI%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7045f039&sv=2)

Based on your discussion with **PayPal**, they will send you an email to let you know that your request is being reviewed. Once you've been approved, the **API** will be marked with a **check mark**, indicating that the **Payouts API** is live.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F8mikZJ8PqZU1Z3XrI3Dn%2Fimg2759_ilethnhd.jpeg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=197e71f0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FMgoBP4nhxkeDvDCrG5e1%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=93220314&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/paypal#step-3-create-your-app)

Step 3: Create your app


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to **Apps & Credentials,** switch from **Sandbox** to **Live** mode, and then click **Create App**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F7VCmVI2JUyhi9PbVdU4C%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5968e61c&sv=2)

Keep in mind that you must switch to **Live** mode. If you don't, the credentials attained from the app you create will be deemed **invalid**.

Next, fill in the app name (**BixGrow**) and click **Create App**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fwul8JgGZ9nW0XvQaTZZ1%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8eae109b&sv=2)

Now, you will see your **Client ID** and **Secret**, which will be used in the next step.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F2hgRR41udw5eDb0uxhfb%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=22ed3637&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/paypal#step-4-integrate-with-bixgrow)

Step 4: Integrate with BixGrow


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Return to **BixGrow** \> **Settings** \> **Integration** and click the **Connect** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FpRRVHATptfB8IVt2EmOE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a01e02a-14ac-4ac8-b41a-4bbda330dd1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94f117f9&sv=2)

Then, enter the **Client ID** and **Secret** in **Step 3** and create a strong **Payment Password** that will be required to fill in when you process payments. It secures your credentials since we don't have access to your money. To keep your payouts safe, every access to your **Payouts API** will require this **Payment Password**.

This is where you set up a **Payment Password** _dedicated to_ _**PayPal Payouts**_ _inside_ _**BixGrow**_ _only_. Do **NOT** input your **PayPal** account's password.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FTy1xTjbJJcV76TEChyHN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De96db558-1342-4feb-adf4-42fe8d24a64e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d69abdcf&sv=2)

For your own payment security, we don't have access to your **Payment Password**, nor can we retrieve it when it's lost or forgotten. If you don't remember it, you'll have to **re-configure** your **Payouts API** with **BixGrow** by entering your **Client ID & Secret** again and setting up a new **Payment Password**.

Also, tick on the two boxes to agree that our app will securely store your information and use these credentials to transfer money outside of your **PayPal** account. Finally, click **Save**.

[PreviousMailchimp](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/mailchimp)
[NextStaff accounts](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/staff-accounts)

Last updated 5 months ago

# Manual Payment | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

You can manually pay affiliates using a third-party app such as an i-banking app, Google Pay, Stripe,... etc. This method requires you to initiate the payment outside and then return to **BixGrow** to mark the commission as paid.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z/manual-payment#a.-manual-payment-process)

A. Manual payment process


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**1.** The **merchant** selects manual payment method(s) [**here**](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/add-payment-methods)
. All payment methods except PayPal integration and Store Credit are considered manual payment methods and are **NOT AUTOMATED**.

**2.** **BixGrow** provides corresponding information forms (see [**example**](https://docs.bixgrow.com/settings/payment#1.-payment-method)
) for **affiliates** to fill in.

**3.** The **merchant** generates a payout and uses the given payment information to transfer **affiliates** their corresponding commission (for example, in a bank app for Bank Transfers).

**4.** The **merchant** returns to **BixGrow** and marks the payout as paid (see below for how).

**5.** **BixGrow** sends the affiliate an email notification of the payout including transaction details.

**BixGrow** only supports collecting required affiliates' information so that you can make payments outside the app. You **CAN'T** make in-app payments except with PayPal integration and Store Credit.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z/manual-payment#b.-make-manual-payments)

B. Make manual payments


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is **steps 3 and 4** where you can make a manual payment and mark the commission as paid.

You'll see a **Mark as paid** button here. When you click it, a pop-up will appear with the commission amount and the payment info that the affiliate has given you.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FTTrig401DdEXGzt4Rx6B%252FScreenshot_50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9dde2832-86d8-4862-8859-5933cacea3f3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f6a3fb6d&sv=2)

Now using this information, please transfer the commission amount via your third-party payment app.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FvL4JQTX1PiXrW2dS628f%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f60eb487&sv=2)

Once you've made the transaction, return to the payout pop-up, check the _**I guarantee that this payout has been transferred outside of BixGrow**_ box, and click the **Mark as paid** button to confirm that the payout has been made.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fu1rkneNwnDYglEfodJVn%252FScreenshot_51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec7acc12-4079-49a7-863f-07244740aef5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5738384&sv=2)

All paid commissions will be shown in the **History** tab. You can view the payout details again here.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F1I5iM9TDnDbMZR3p68Vk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D529f6645-23bd-4b1b-a189-a47d2102b4bd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b13fb6f&sv=2)

When a commission is paid, it will appear in the **Affiliate dashboard** as follows:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fj3bLAgOY4ps471vqzvFT%252FScreenshot_53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa114be3-c4b5-475e-a335-59e521603243&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4739992a&sv=2)

[NextIn-app Payment](https://docs.bixgrow.com/payouts/how-to-make-payments-a-z/in-app-payment)

# Embed your affiliate portal into the store | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

A tutorial video can be found here:

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/embed-on-the-storefront#step-1-create-a-shopify-page-template)

**Step 1: Create a Shopify page template**

Go to **Settings** \> **Affiliate portal** \> **Embed into your store** in the app. This will redirect you to your **Shopify theme editor**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FCqXOyQT8Na6jncWSUM2K%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D647550d0-73a5-4e91-92d5-318dd63de23d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=152aa464&sv=2)

In the theme editor, navigate to **Pages** \> **Create template**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FghvmR1uEJzkK1aVSZ7HY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D006bf65f-fc8c-46bf-9f9d-f81255b1e06e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f51756fc&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F7VGdGWbUBVxcvE59svzf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da31d167f-e706-489f-9560-8e89876d74e1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3b82f1f&sv=2)

Enter a name for your new template (e.g., _Become an affiliate_). Choose **Default page** as the base, then click **Create template**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FfNK5GtHEGlbjK9Ci5Nf4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad11c6b3-b208-4ef0-966b-ce3366b276fd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d307e40f&sv=2)

If needed, **hide the Default page section** to make the page blank.

Go to **Add section** \> **Apps**, then select the **BixGrow signup page** template. Adjust the page’s margins as necessary.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FHkkicEWZvLkDiPVV7Kil%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5b0f658-13c2-4ee1-a59c-a0e1bf0f5bae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2485718a&sv=2)

Click the **app block’s name** to access optional settings:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FKTEcPrWKKFYPhAsiXZ59%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6ab8a237-4875-4fc4-afcb-2794c25c885f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c1a24128&sv=2)

Select the affiliate **program sign-up link** to display on the page. This is useful if you have multiple programs and wish to embed a different page from the default one.

Click **Save** to apply your changes.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FFIvyW9TNIb4kLOjv57Zu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db795ce4d-587c-451a-a7b6-6bbff8ba5c59&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e4d7e6e1&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/embed-on-the-storefront#step-2-add-a-shopify-page-using-the-created-template)

**Step 2: Add a Shopify Page Using the Created Template**

Go to your **Shopify admin** \> **Online store** \> **Pages,** click **Add page**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fv0PD7McW5HOU9c7jmlh3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a591c6b-404a-44d0-bd25-79b32e197276&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=608e1a86&sv=2)

Enter a title for your page (e.g., _Become an affiliate_).

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FJaa7t8utOdcrjzEYb7vm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6db10d5-fe08-416d-9bec-8c035d10eba6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b566c1f1&sv=2)

Under **Theme template**, choose the template you just created and then click **Save**.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/embed-on-the-storefront#step-3-add-the-created-page-to-your-stores-menu)

**Step 3: Add the created page to your store's menu**

Navigate to **Shopify admin** \> **Content** \> **Menus**.

Click on the **menu** where you'd like to display the page (e.g., Main Menu or Footer Menu).

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F1ifT5YLiSgSVwyr0Sc7S%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6909e35-03b0-475d-99c8-e6423a382add&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8eac40e0&sv=2)

Click **Add menu item**:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FuWAMUC4oEmHB6Yt2f7N7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9fdac2ca-da65-43b6-b1e6-7ecdf5fe8fef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=75b6d583&sv=2)

Enter a name for the menu item (e.g., _Affiliate Program_). Under **Link**, select **Pages** \> **\[Your created page\]**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FHlIC9NiRpxDCOVyjIcZs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13a002f8-a1e4-4991-ad7e-360165289739&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d84be5e&sv=2)

Click **Add**, then click **Save** to confirm.

This is a sample **Affiliate sign-up page** that is displayed directly on the storefront:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FUUtEDGP3p9DyBzttqSZ3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D045597d1-aabb-4c1e-878f-cd39a46d18d3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f4ac268e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/embed-on-the-storefront#step-4-link-the-embedded-signup-and-landing-pages-optional)

Step 4: Link the Embedded Signup & Landing Pages (Optional)

By default, clicking the **Sign Up** button in your affiliate portal will redirect users to the **default sign-up page**.

To change this to the **embedded version**, first you copy the **link to the embedded sign-up page** (created in Step 2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Fq4pzrCh6T46b4VyPkvZu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c30507a-7835-47f3-8fd0-0b86cb2df778&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5288f63f&sv=2)

Repeat the same steps to embed **Landing page** to your store.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FFe6BKxBRvRR7NGONChPx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2cb8c92-00e8-42d8-a377-5afb43676326&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec2ed109&sv=2)

In the app settings, paste the link copied into the **Sign-up button’s link** field.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F60slgjkfC0W8PDVgImH8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D576742a6-bdff-4dce-beba-2f08f0bb8861&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e1ab46de&sv=2)

This ensures users stay on your storefront when signing up.

[PreviousDisplay your affiliate portal on the storefront](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/display-on-the-storefront)
[NextGuide affiliates with Program Directory](https://docs.bixgrow.com/affiliate-portal/program-directory)

# Widget | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F47LAnMhsAxVs309samcR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ed77e6d-c3c8-429f-b984-03baa7b21bbe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1128b0b9&sv=2)

You can customize the **Widget**'s content and appearance for both steps: Before and after someone signs up as an advocate.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FpO0647CzdHCJPjHPCYa0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8be20535-8c9c-4fb0-9e8f-95447b73bf0c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6dec4ba7&sv=2)

# Klaviyo | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

**Klaviyo** is a marketing automation software for e-commerce. You'll be able to fully automate your marketing campaigns and boost them with the support of your affiliates after the integration procedure is complete.

A tutorial video can be found here.

In order to integrate, you must first get the **Klaviyo API key** of your **Klaviyo** account.

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/klaviyo#id-1.-sign-up-or-log-in-to-your-klaviyo-account)

1\. Sign up or log in to [your Klaviyo account](https://www.klaviyo.com/login)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F63jYcSRmYwzJ17uB5izh%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3636a938&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/klaviyo#id-2.-create-your-list)

2\. Create your list

In your **Klaviyo** dashboard, click the **Lists and Segments** tab > **Create list/segment** to add a new **list**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FvkwxJVJNKxQvYqqXjqvN%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b7744ac&sv=2)

Next, select **List**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fcy0L7JiFMgFAKkOm2PX0%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7b17a2d&sv=2)

Finally, fill in the list name and click **Create List**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FBgXk9NOWHAcJdYzrg4l7%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=91be42a6&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/klaviyo#id-3.-get-the-klaviyo-api-key)

**3\. Get the Klaviyo API Key**

To get the API Key, click on your **Account**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fb1EqZOQsMJ9ZZlMkvayc%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=757b4a31&sv=2)

In the **Settings** tab, click **API Keys.**

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fcd8fKNPaA1ya07TqaALw%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8aa22000&sv=2)

If you haven't created any **API keys** in your account, create a new one by clicking on **Create Private API Key**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FAP2ZRxJMgdfQmtzFMHP3%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=62f2206b&sv=2)

Next, fill in the API Key name, select **Full Access Key**, and click **Create**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fmr9lCpjdDQKLV55gzSY8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7fd9a26a&sv=2)

Now, copy the API Key.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FiWWJiXfkhtrdSxdgASZ0%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fb8a27af&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/klaviyo#id-4.-integrate-with-bixgrow)

4\. Integrate with BixGrow

Go back to **BixGrow** > **Settings** \> **Integration** \> **Klaviyo** and click **Connect**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252Ful1Gbq2OrXIY7Mc6EDkS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e2e1cf1-4832-4580-94df-15b206c6a674&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c57e05c&sv=2)

Paste the key into the **API Key** box and click **Next**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FStfOcusf0oJptyBXo9yT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D731a3f9b-d89a-462c-b5b4-423fc5b40f06&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca253c86&sv=2)

It's recommended that you choose **Only sync if the affiliate is approved** to avoid sending marketing emails to pending or denied affiliate accounts.

Finally, select the **List** you've just created and click **Save and Sync** to complete the integration.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FFOx4dn1XsWHNHB94UYvP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80a02083-c2b7-4b1a-b545-004fbaded44c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9fc3d37&sv=2)

[PreviousIntegration](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration)
[NextMailchimp](https://docs.bixgrow.com/other-settings/integration/mailchimp)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Custom Domain | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

By default, your affiliate portal exists on our subdomain (e.g. _yourdomain.bixgrow.com_). Our **PRO** plan allows you to use a **Custom Domain** instead (e.g. _affiliate.yourdomain.com_) so that you're not only able to remove “bixgrow.com” from the URL and completely white-label **BixGrow**, but also display your affiliate portal in a more personalized and branded way.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FuNYG2xpF7snpc0LybpFl%2FCustom%2520Domain%2520For%2520PRO%2520Users.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85a807d7&sv=2)

There are some preparations you can make before contacting us so that the process will take the least time:

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/custom-domain#id-1-create-a-cname-record)

**1\. Create a CNAME record**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a CNAME for your desired domain (e.g. affiliate.yourdomain.com) that points to partners.bixgrow.com.

Your CNAME must point to affiliate.yourdomain.com and **NOT** your Shopify domain (e.g. yourdomain.com) because each domain can only point to **ONE** site.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/custom-domain#id-2-check-your-cname-record)

Example

**Shopify**[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/custom-domain#shopify)

If your domain name registrar is Shopify, please go to **Shopify** \> **Settings** \> **Domains** and click on it.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FgIs1MvVTlBZwDMnbRtj2%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec882923&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FlVnEzO4rR1wpNMZuY7Xx%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=82b9487a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FVhogdmM7pfxNoRFeLFia%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f67c8ba1&sv=2)

Here, add a CNAME record named affiliate that points to partners.bixgrow.com.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F0IbXkfKobtwyEAxLFhHg%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7801e65b&sv=2)

**GoDaddy**[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/custom-domain#godaddy)

If your domain name registrar is GoDaddy, please go to **GoDaddy** \> **Account Settings** > **My Products** and click on it.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fmh9VjpG0DffmFMnjVB1f%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a749d08&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F1Mr5ov88blAtqtkkfFJM%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e585e9d5&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FT1ogzQQpUHJRXIjQaD2r%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e0d00d9&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FO8PCE9PJwIGC32WxNS5p%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aac36236&sv=2)

Here, add a CNAME record named affiliate whose value is partners.bixgrow.com.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FJnb0ELNzbV4o7iJHGJlS%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46babf8e&sv=2)

Namecheap[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/custom-domain#namecheap)

If your domain name registrar is Namecheap, please go to **Namecheap** \> **Domain List** and click on it.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FEqo1DwKOX5ulhjuYJeAg%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ab11555c&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FtgtQ76H7LK0CRXty2KAO%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a62c80a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FCiP5dN2G56HQ5XgwVOdv%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72419bae&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FkidXsHWmZNe4WKS7zE1c%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=235ec335&sv=2)

Here, add a CNAME record hosted by affiliate whose value is partners.bixgrow.com.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FVAJR4QaWO1iPQvPhnHq7%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b2bfa8c&sv=2)

Name.com[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/custom-domain#name.com)

If your domain name registrar is Name.com, please go to **Name.com** \> **My Domains** and click on it.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FB4INvfp7NCJnuml5UB1c%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=348aabeb&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fc8hHcpzDmVGMIibVqcue%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=66e8a3c3&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FIE67kLHRFnI9u5HQDs5w%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d988b228&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F5vB0cnGsNvfCYFnDSCQQ%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c27dfb2&sv=2)

Here, add a CNAME record hosted by affiliate whose answer is partners.bixgrow.com.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fvy3BfoSDkQnOmXxuVxBf%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=914bc515&sv=2)

**Cloudflare**[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/custom-domain#cloudflare)

If your domain name registrar is Cloudflare, please go to **Cloudflare** \> **Websites** and click on it.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FugjjzeqHqFJE4D7y1TX3%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea7c62e8&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FYHdepUCVFXvYBQaw89Eu%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98f2cf15&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FQXkJlp3CjFSUFvLjn5de%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=575a1f0c&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FOLqMtp21IWFGp9R0rrpW%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c317061&sv=2)

Here, add a CNAME record named affiliate whose target is partners.bixgrow.com.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FybEphxz30XW0WLMKGPII%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3c7c3b8e&sv=2)

If you already added a CNAME whose Proxy status is **Proxied** and not **DNS only**, please edit it here:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fp9Vvvy1IqYJntPdXsafx%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=65f4393e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fz0OcfFWmvuxO6ayYx4NC%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2d7e66ba&sv=2)

Please note that DNS changes can take up to 48 hours to apply.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/custom-domain#id-2-check-your-cname-record-1)

**2\. Check your CNAME record**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use a CNAME lookup tool (like [this](https://mxtoolbox.com/CNAMELookup.aspx)
) to double-check your CNAME.

✅ Your CNAME is **correct**:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FCrSUvLWkIeqSTRqmdNAd%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea503216&sv=2)

⛔️ Your CNAME is **incorrect**:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F6OjzXAEKOM7GhYfks4Y1%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a038cc41&sv=2)

If you're having trouble setting up the CNAME, please contact your domain name registrar for further assistance.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/custom-domain#id-3.-contact-us)

**3\. Contact us**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you've completed the preparation steps above and your CNAME record is correct, contact **our Developer team** and we'll finish the setup for you! It generally takes up just a couple of minutes.

#### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/branding/custom-domain#example)

Example

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FLpYkeW5nbvuRo9UoHFqu%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c1336836&sv=2)

# Custom Page | BixGrow: Affiliate Marketing

1.  [Enable Custom Page](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#enable-custom-page)
    
2.  [Custom Page design](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#custom-page-design)
    
3.  [Create a Shopify page template](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#create-a-shopify-page-template)
    
4.  [Add a page on Shopify for the created template](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#add-a-page-on-shopify-for-created-template)
    
5.  [Add created Custom Page to your store's menu](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#add-created-custom-page-to-your-stores-menu)
    

A tutorial video can be found here.

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#enable-custom-page)

Enable Custom Page


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To enable the **Custom Page**, you must first click this **Turn on** button.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FEVddT4d0hORoHRVKA0dd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f93644b-8bdc-495e-a5dd-21130d19c842&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3f8f0321&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#custom-page-design)

Custom Page design


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is where you can design the **Custom Page** displayed to both advocates and their friends (if selected).

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FvZfpk64MmtDEUIUDLHjW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf3452ca-1dee-4a32-b888-976e4bb678d2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=443e0d25&sv=2)

You can freely customize the page's appearance and content. Any changes will be reflected in the right column's preview display.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FetsM3EOQjwz2tGB2Z9vx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63c1d3e9-9d9f-4666-98fa-f5206eb90585&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1fd358a2&sv=2)

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#display-custom-page-on-your-storefront)

Display Custom Page on your storefront


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#create-a-shopify-page-template)

Create a Shopify page template

You must first create a new Shopify page template. Please go to your Shopify account > **Online store** > **Themes** \> **Customize**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FGoCQmRQ34zcqnz7ahPvh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1732fd1c-a0b8-4ba1-aa16-541884c291f2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72c8dffc&sv=2)

On **Home page**, **select Pages** \> **Create template**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FHzm9AXJ6jybWbkZrNYCM%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72ab936f&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FD7FgSqbpOSNz1TzUgYxq%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2964ae7b&sv=2)

Now enter a name for the template, choose **Default page** and click **Create template**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2Fgw8ZYRLpgSWFKTJTAUfu%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d305a680&sv=2)

Next, hide that **Default page**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FB30SrHosq3dN85UXfIxg%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=465d0b44&sv=2)

In **Add section** > **Apps**, select the "BixGrow referral page" template and edit the page's margin. Click **Save** when you're done.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2F8ZORm9v8BzXh5W6O4yI4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6feff894&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%2Fblobs%2FKxRCHTqyDlbkFjqRw5m2%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a76217&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#add-a-page-on-shopify-for-created-template)

Add a page on Shopify for created template

Now return to **Online store** > **Pages**. Click **Add page**, then enter a title for the page. Under **Theme template**, select the template you've just created above.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FpIgDNgMaJ3kKJ5iLxTNq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6471351a-9e5e-455b-b18e-4a53c188ac9c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d904029b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FPzXKucaUC4WsXJqluvW9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3022efb9-990e-4c82-a1fc-64563306a7bb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1f893e3e&sv=2)

Then, click **Save**.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F1irPOlM4FaXc3743Gemd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19c8b502-88f4-4193-882a-d6a4166f0f02&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9231b651&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bixgrow.com/referral/attract-advocates-to-sign-up-for-your-program/custom-page#add-created-custom-page-to-your-stores-menu)

Add created Custom Page to your store's menu

Finally, let's add the created **Custom page** to your store's menu. Return to your Shopify account > **Content** > **Menus**. Click on your header menu (usually named **Main menu**).

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FjPDb76wSOIk3GgPBwvBO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D76734521-948f-42f4-ae7b-cedfa8164fe2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b6af4c4&sv=2)

Now click **Add menu item**. Then, enter a label for the page and select **Pages** \> the page you just created above.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FYI7EacGWIEE83wUiJplj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c6af06c-bf4f-4d61-a139-fc650df60fae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=682bebe8&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FYtHTVu8Uo0XOB5EERoMc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9747127b-09ac-4cd8-940f-82c6b212284c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=37aca347&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252F8HU0jUBN9mzsc76fa47y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a39b2d4-9051-4509-b68b-16d1945cb73e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d0734028&sv=2)

Finally, click **Add** and then **Save** to update your changes.

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FLNFfmZJ7ozmw46TQBdsK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8919d9e5-c8ab-4236-9105-1da338d2d36b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=480a68fa&sv=2)

This is a sample **Custom Page** that is displayed directly on the storefront:

![](https://docs.bixgrow.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1262132294-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F8I1FvDPwi1VP7QixsjAS%252Fuploads%252FuttmCpKq2zT27qpcWPtw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De86c0895-9727-4de9-99c4-c32a06dadbcc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26a962d3&sv=2)
